Chen Diaoyuan and Ruan Zhaochang Arrive in Wuhu

Chen Will Go to Anqing After Inspecting the Troops

Wuhu Dispatch: Chen Diaoyuan, the chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, came to Anhui to take office and preside over the Anhui government with various provincial committee members. He arrived in Wuhu at 12 noon today (6th) from Nanjing on the Anfeng charter boat. Wuhu has the 55th and 57th Division troops newly arrived from the front, Chen made a special trip to shore to inspect. Those who followed included the 55th Division Commander Ruan Zhaochang, the Chief of Staff of the Reserve Headquarters Liu Weiliang, the Adjutant General Hao Guoxi, and more than ten people. All circles here had pre-organized a welcoming party at the Jiangkou Zhonghua Hotel. After Chen landed ashore and rested for a while, he attended the welcoming party of all circles at one o'clock in the afternoon. The county party committee Zhang Shuye spoke on behalf of all circles. It was roughly stated that Chairman Chen was a loyal and brave comrade of this party. In the past, he had considerable achievements in governing Anhui and Shandong. It is especially worthy of the public's welcome to come to Anhui again to suppress the rebels and eliminate the obstacles of the revolution, and it is hoped that Chen will pay attention to the following two things: 1. Eliminate the bandits and communists so that the people of Anhui can live and work in peace. 2. Strive to complete the training of the government and complete local autonomy. Chen Diaoyuan then stood up and replied, roughly stating that Diaoyuan was very ashamed to be welcomed by all circles when he came to Anhui again. Recalling the Republic of China in the seventeenth year, he once served the people of Anhui, but he was immediately transferred to Shandong without any achievements. However, he has never forgotten the people of Anhui for a day. Now I dare to tell you the principle of not aiming high and not rushing. (1) In the political aspect, the only key is to never increase the burden on the people of Anhui. Everything should be done according to the amount of income. Now that the training period has arrived, construction is especially important. The automobile roads from Anqing to Hefei and from Guangde to Tunxi should be actively completed, and all revolutionary obstacles should be eliminated in the shortest possible time to implement local autonomy. (2) In terms of public security, the Communist Party is a hidden danger, and bandits are only a superficial disease. The Communist Party carries out its destructive behavior everywhere. The destruction of the Jingdezhen porcelain industry in Jiangxi this time is a clear proof. The communists on the border of Jiangxi and Anhui are extremely rampant, and the communists in southern Anhui are also a hidden danger. However, the neighboring danger must be eliminated first before this province can be consolidated. It has now been decided to transfer the Ruan Zhaochang department of the 55th Division to the border of Jiangxi to suppress the communists. One brigade of the Yue Shengxuan department of the 57th Division will be left in this province to work hard to eliminate bandits. Diaoyuan will be fully responsible for the public security in this province, and the people of Anhui can rest assured. (3) In terms of military affairs, the Fan Xiji department of the 46th Division has now been stationed in Bengbu, and the Ruan Zhaochang department of the 55th Division is continuing to depart to Jiangxi. The Yue Shengxuan department of the 57th Division is stationed in central and southern Anhui. The above three divisions and two brigades have been instructed by the central government to be commanded by Diaoyuan. However, after the war, the army must be greatly reorganized, and military discipline and discipline must be paid more attention to. I hope that the people of Anhui will not abandon and assist. Then I will be very grateful. Because the time is rushed today, it is inconvenient to talk more. I will find a good meeting in the future. After the speech, he immediately left his seat with Ruan Zhaochang and took a car to the Taikoo Wharf to inspect the troops of the 55th and 57th Divisions who had already arrived in Wuhu, and gave speeches to comfort them. Then he boarded the ship to meet the heads of various agencies and representatives of various groups, including Zhu Dian, a homeowner of Wanchun Township, and Zhang Yanghe, who presented the farmers in the township gathering to protest rent parades and demonstrations. Chen immediately ordered County Magistrate Yu Yuying to handle it strictly, and those who disobey would be shot. Around 4 o'clock, the visitors resigned one after another, and Anfeng then set sail for the province. Commander Ruan of the 55th Division will temporarily stay in Wuhu to wait for his troops to complete their departure before going to Jiangxi to command (November 6th).

Local News

Songjiang

Bandits Trying to Escape by Swimming Shot Dead: Recently, the bandit Xiao Jinqian (namely Li Lanyu) secretly returned from Shanghai and hid in the Huxingdang area, plotting wrongdoing. Chen Zhankui, the chief of the 11th District and director of the Songshan Fengjing Party, government, military, and police joint defense office, received a report from an informant. He immediately went to the area with the militia and police to arrest the bandit the day before. After the bandit learned of it, he carried a gun and resisted arrest. Because the ammunition was exhausted, he was captured alive by the militia and police. When crossing the boat in Yuhuitou, the bandit suddenly fled into the water. The militia and police fired shots to pursue, and the bandit was shot dead. Yesterday morning, the county government was requested to transfer to the county court's chief investigator to send personnel to Fengjing to inspect.

Songyi's Winter Rent Collected at 85%: The late rice planted in various districts of the county is about to be harvested, but due to continuous rain, work cannot be started, and there is a risk of rice germination. Yesterday, the Education Bureau, the Rent Collection Office, and the Property Office invited representatives from various party, government, and local organizations to discuss the quality of rent collection. In previous years, there were slight differences in the north and south of Pudong. This year, it was decided that the harvest was abundant and there was no distinction in grades. Rent was collected at 85% uniformly, that is, 8.5 dou (a unit of dry measure) per stone (another unit of dry measure) was actually collected, and the rent was converted at the market value.

Suzhou

Parricide Case Scheduled for Trial: Sun Liansheng, a native of Nantong, from Qijiaqiao, Zhabei, Shanghai, colluded with Qiu Shuntao, Qiu Lansheng, Ji Shuangquan and others to kill his adoptive father Sun Laowu in July of this year. The Shanghai District Court sentenced Sun Liansheng and Ji Shuangquan to death, Qiu Shuntao to life imprisonment, and Qiu Lansheng to 15 years' imprisonment. The convicts refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the High Court, which was transferred to Suzhou on October 25 to await trial. The High Court has now scheduled the hearing for the afternoon of the 17th of this month.

Kidnapping Suspect Released on Bail: The 14th team of the Public Security Bureau and the guerrilla team opened fire with bandits in Shenjiagang outside the West Gate of Wujiang a few days ago and rescued the kidnapped boatman Qian Asan and arrested the suspects Gu Yun, Sun Daocai, Yan Zhongshan and others. After the district leader interrogated, he (Qian Asan) testified. Last night (7th), Shen, the district head, interrogated and proved that Qian Asan was indeed a hostage, and that Sun Daocai and others were indeed suspects. Yesterday (8th), Zhang Changshou went to the district to bail Qian Asan, and Xue Xueqiao and Zhang Xiaoxian went to the district to present a report to bail Sun Daocai. As for Gu Yun, Yan Zhongshan and other four people, they were ordered to find a proper bail for release. The guerrillas rescued two wine boats of Zhang Tonghe and Jin Xiexing wine shops in Hengjingdu Village, Tai Temple Port, with a total of 133. Yesterday, the industry's Zhang Jiyuan bailed them out.

Night Sailing Encountered Bandits Robbing: Around 3:00 p.m. the day before yesterday (7th), there was a night sailing boat from Guangfu Mudu passing through the area near Dongkuatang outside the Xumen (Suzhou city gate). Suddenly, eight bandits armed with five pistols and three short knives blocked the boat and robbed it. More than 400 yuan was robbed and they escaped. Afterwards, boat owner Sun Renfu reported to the Fifth Branch of Mudu and reported to the county for investigation.

Four-County Joint Defense Meeting: Wuxian, Wujiang, Kunshan, and Qingpu counties will hold a joint defense meeting. It has been decided that the joint defense meeting will be held at the Wuxian County Government on the afternoon of the 14th of this month to discuss winter defense measures.

Owner of a Paper Shop Taken to Shanghai: Yesterday morning (8th) at 8:00 a.m., Xu Songshan and Li Zhongtian, detectives from the Fourth District of the Shanghai Wusong Maritime Provincial Public Security Bureau, came to Suzhou to the Songyuanshun Paper Shop at No. 6 Huangfang Bridge, Xinqiao Gate. Fengxian

Younger Brother Abducts Brother's Wife, Uncle Implicated: Zhang Xingsheng, a farmer from the 18th District, married Wang last spring. Because her husband was away at work and rarely came home, she gradually became adulterous with her husband's younger brother, Amu, like a married couple. Recently, she suddenly learned that her brother had lost his job and was about to return home, so she secretly transported out her small items one after another. On the first day of this month, she took her brother's wife out without a trace. Yesterday, Xingsheng returned to the village and learned about it. He searched everywhere but found nothing. However, for some unknown reason, he mistakenly believed that his younger brother had an affair with his wife and fled under the instigation of his uncle, a monk. Yesterday, he went to make a fuss and swallowed raw tobacco to show his determination to fight. Fortunately, he was rescued by the neighbors, and his uncle personally guaranteed on the spot that he would catch up within a month.

Telegram to Stop Exceeding Land Price: The land tax levied on the county's land this year, including the regular tax, has exceeded 1% of the land price. Yesterday, the County Supervisory Committee submitted it for discussion and immediately consulted the Executive Committee to send a letter to the county to stop it. At the same time, all sectors of the local community also read and deducted it due to the excessive burden. It is heard that the county financial and land departments will convene a local temporary meeting in the next few days to collect and distribute the reduction in accordance with the previous precedent.

Construction Fee Reduced by Half: The county government is currently investigating that during the tenure of the former county magistrate Hong, the government organized various agencies to solicit construction donations from local gentry and wealthy people in order to reorganize the Nanchiao municipal administration. The total amount of special donations was more than 3,400 yuan. Later, due to turnover, the government was suspended, so it was not collected. Now, due to the need to build municipal bridges, it has been decided to collect half of the original amount donated by each household. It has been entrusted to the Property Office and the Construction Bureau to send personnel to handle it yesterday.

Wujiang

Prison Guard Arrested for Malpractice: Wujiang County Prison Guard Wang Kaiqi was secretly reported. After the county government sent personnel to secretly investigate and confirmed that he had embezzled prisoners' rations and collected fees privately, the county stopped and arrested the prison guard. The county magistrate was temporarily appointed by the Wuxian County magistrate to concurrently act as the director of the county public security bureau and judicial affairs, Peng Hong, to wait for the High Court to send personnel to take over.

Private Transportation of Rice Confiscated in Pingwang: The Yuantaifeng rice store in Pingwang Town transported 85 stone of rice out of the border and was seized. The county government decided that the rice would be confiscated and a fine of 300 yuan would be imposed. The store refused to accept the ruling and planned to appeal to the province.

Wuxi

Old Grain Embezzlement Case in Chunyun Continues in Liyang: It is learned that in the initial review of the old grain embezzlement case, Jiang Suoming, a citizen of Liyang County, and others filed a complaint with the Civil and Financial Affairs Office accusing Cao Qingyun's son Cao Cong and Lu Wen, Chen Ronglin and others of colluding to embezzle and steal grain. The Financial Affairs Office has instructed Inspector Shen Dingjiu to conduct a strict investigation and handle it together with this case. According to the people of Liyang, when Zhang Quan was the county magistrate and director of the Finance Bureau, Cao and Pan Bin, the deputy director of the Finance Bureau, Zou Hanliang, the chief of the levy section, Cheng Lin, the director of land tax, and Tu Zhouqing, etc., took the opportunity when the Big Sword Society bandit Cai Laowu trampled on the county town to handle the land tax. The Finance Office approved the appointment of the Director of the Jintan Finance Bureau to come to Liyang for investigation. However, he returned one day after arriving in Liyang. At this time, Zhang Quan summoned Pan Bin, Lin Hanliang and Secretary Liu to open the Grain Book Room and secretly ordered Shen Zhiqing, the current director of land tax, to hide the grain books. Before long, Zhang's dismissal order was issued, and he ordered the staff of the Land Tax Office and the officials of the Finance Bureau to sell this grain book at a price. Zou Hanliang promised to raise eight or nine thousand yuan the next day before handing over the 120,000 yuan of grain books, and the case came to an end. However, the other day, Zhang Quan suddenly came to the province in the name of a qualified police officer representative of the Jiangsu Province Examination to petition for a thorough investigation of this case. Therefore, the truth of this case is really confusing and outsiders cannot understand it. The Chairman of the Provincial Government Ye has decided to transfer Zheng Chengyuan and others to the court for interrogation yesterday (8th).

Doushan Xihetou Accuses Robbery Again: Xie Shouxuan, a Wuxi citizen, recently hired workers to build a wall on his father's tomb in Doushan Xihetou, the sixth district (Tianxia City), and sent his family member Xie Zhongshan (50 years old) to the village to supervise the construction. Xie arrived in the village and lived in the home of He Renbao, who was guarding the tomb. Around 12 o'clock last night, more than ten bandits suddenly came, each armed with guns and knives, broke into the house, imprisoned He Renbao and his wife in the room and did not allow them to move, tied up Xie Zhongshan with ropes and beat him severely. Then they searched at will, took their loot and left. After the incident, only Xie Zhongshan's purse was stolen, containing more than 20 yuan.

A Murder Case Occurred in Bezhakou: Resident Zeng Haishan, a native of Hubei, 44 years old, who resided in the 12th factory in Bezhakou near Beimen outside the county town, served as a training instructor in the Jiangyin County Government Patrol Team two years ago. He was dismissed last year and came to Wuxi to specialize in selling soil for profit. Around 1 a.m. last night, a thug holding a kitchen knife suddenly broke into the door and went straight to Haishan's room. At that time, Haishan and his wife Yao Laoer (20 years old) were sleeping soundly. The thug raised the kitchen knife and chopped Haishan's head, face, left and right arms more than 20 times. Suddenly, blood was splashing and he was unconscious. His wife Yao Laoer saw this and immediately stepped forward to snatch the knife. The thug kicked her to the ground and took the opportunity to escape. After the incident, Yao Laoer carried the injured Zeng Haishan to Ma Mingshang Brothers Hospital for treatment. However, due to excessive blood loss, his life was in danger. It is heard that Zeng Haishan's wife Yao Laoer originally had her own husband and Zeng funded her divorce. A few days ago, they quarreled over the unequal distribution of profits among their partners in the soil business. Therefore, the cause of this bloodshed is nothing more than adultery and revenge.

New Developments in Consecutive Robbery and Kidnapping Cases: Five families in Dengjiawan and Xiaoqiaotou in the 22nd district of the county were robbed by bandits on October 6, and seven victims were kidnapped. Except for the victims Ling Rendda and Ling Baoxian who were released by the bandits two days after being kidnapped, the remaining five people, You Junde, Ling Azhang, and Ling Jiansheng, were still in the bandit den and repeatedly sent letters demanding huge amounts of ransom. Recently, Ling Rendda entrusted a friend, A, to go to the location agreed upon in the bandit's letter to contact the bandit's representative. As a result, the victim's side first sent 3,000 yuan. The bandit's representative collected the full amount and said that Ling Jiansheng among the hostages could reduce 5,000 yuan, and the rest could also be reduced as appropriate. You Junde originally demanded 50,000 yuan and agreed to reduce 10,000 yuan. After A returned to his hometown, he informed Ling Rendda to raise money to redeem them. Then, the day before yesterday, he suddenly received the bandit's fourth letter, roughly saying that the 3,000 yuan received before was a meeting fee, limited to a certain place to meet with the victims on the 10th of this month. After reading the letter, they raised the money and still entrusted A to take the money to meet at the agreed address yesterday to redeem the tickets.

Changzhou

Kidnapping and Robbery in Jinjiatang, Fifth District: On the evening of the 5th, six bandits suddenly came to the home of Jin Quanda in Jinjiatang, Jingshan Township, Fifth District of Wuxian, each armed with guns and weapons. They searched the room arbitrarily. Because they did not get silver coins, they kidnapped Jin Zibao and left, with no whereabouts.

A Robbery Occurred in Zhoujiagang, Fu Guo: Around 12 o'clock on the evening of the 6th, seven bandits suddenly came to the home of Zhou Jipei in Zhoujiagang outside the North Gate of Wuxian County. They were all wearing blue short shirts, wearing headscarves and holding flashlights and pistols. They entered the room and robbed silver coins, soft valuables, and miscellaneous items.

Jiangyin

Provincial Order to Investigate the Sheng Family's Rebellious Property: Last year, the National Government ordered the provincial government to order the counties of Suzhou and Changzhou to investigate and determine the amount of Sheng Xingsun's rebellious property within their borders and implement its seizure. Jiangyin had already investigated and seized a total of 13,000 and 9.2% shares of the Jimin Junda Two Pawnshops. Now, the National Government, according to a secret report, states that the Zhuo Yuan Yichuang Foundation in Changzhou has a shortage of funds and the manager of the confiscated Qianfeng Rice Store has the hope of embezzling it. Although it specifically refers to Changzhou, other counties, such as real estate pawnshops, are responsible for the safekeeping of this confiscated property. If there is any shortage, the manager will be questioned. After receiving the order, the provincial government ordered the county magistrates of Suzhou and Changzhou to immediately investigate and report on the sealed property in accordance with the law.

Nantong

Large Band of Pirates Harassing Tonghai: Recently, pirates from Haizhou and Shandong have been fleeing south from Yancheng and harassing the coastal areas of Tonghai and other three counties. The situation is very rampant. There are as many as one hundred and ten men and women who have been kidnapped. The bandit headquarters is located in Jugang Changsha Port. There are a total of 120 pirate ships with approximately 1,000 people. In addition to sending police teams to intercept them, the county magistrates reported to the bandit suppression headquarters for suppression.

Measures to Reorganize Local Taxes: The local financial revenue and expenditure in Tongyi is very insufficient. The county financial reorganization committee has been organized and is underway to reorganize local taxes and donations separately. (1) Add additional tax on stove land and collect it in the same way as people's land. (2) The commissioned merchant undertakes tax and donation using a bidding system. (3) The county government orders the Finance Bureau to reorganize the collection methods.

Collect Sandfield Case Overflows Tidal Flat: In the Liuhai Sha Jisheng case in Nantong, the overflowed tidal flats in the sixth and seventh dams were investigated and clarified by the provincial and central government committees, and all 1,300 mu were approved by the Nantong Education Bureau to receive 60 yuan per mu, and the money was returned to the national treasury. The provincial government ordered County Magistrate Zhang to implement it quickly and produce results as soon as possible.

Stove Field Will Be Promoted to Science: There are a total of 10,225 mu of stove fields in Tongyi. Due to the different administrative jurisdictions, there are many differences in people's stoves. The county administrative meeting decided to submit a request to the Ministry of Finance to upgrade the stove field to science and merge it into the county to benefit administration.

Zhenjiang

County Government Meeting Resolves Dispute over Yushan Beach Land: The Zhenjiang County Government, due to a long-unresolved dispute between the China Merchants Bureau, the Education Bureau's Lifesaving Society, and Runshang School over the Yushan beach land, convened a meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday. First, the representative of the China Merchants Bureau, Jiao Quheng, stated the reasons, roughly claiming that property rights should be based on contracts. In law, both parties should abide by them. When the China Merchants Bureau purchased the Yushan beach land from the Lifesaving Society, the contract clearly stated that it extended north to the riverbank, and any subsequent accretion or erosion would be the responsibility of the practitioner. Now, disregarding the contract is not only unacceptable to the China Merchants Bureau but also likely legally invalid. The Education Bureau, the Lifesaving Society, and Runshang School raised three points: (1) First, investigate whether the contract bears the county seal and the Jingkou Lifesaving Society seal; otherwise, it may be considered a private unauthorized sale and therefore invalid. (2) The contract's end states that any subsequent accretion or erosion is the responsibility of the practitioner. However, the extent of the accretion is not specified, so it cannot be assumed that the right to manage three mu and two fen of land grants unlimited accretion rights. (3) The China Merchants Bureau did not report or claim the accreted land, so it cannot legally manage it. Finally, the representative of the provincial government, Rui Jun, expressed his opinion, also deeming the contract's end clause illegal. First, the China Merchants Bureau sold three mu and two fen and two li of accreted land. If there is much more, does it all belong to the China Merchants Bureau? Second, accreted beach land naturally belongs to the state. How could the writer sell it at that time? It should be revised. The dispute continued until 6:00 PM without resolution, and the meeting adjourned.

Yangzhou

First Wife Seeks Refuge Due to Abuse: Wei Jia, residing in this city and originally from Yangzihe, formerly served at the Tianchang Shikouzhen salt depot. Later, his affair became known to the Tongfuxiang head office, resulting in his dismissal. Wei then took his anger out on his wife, Xu. Xu is the daughter of the late gentry Xu Yiqing and the younger sister of Xu Youqing. Wei resented his wife for not mediating the situation, so he often beat and verbally abused her. Recently, the whipping was excessive, and neighbors, feeling sorry for Xu, rescued her and sent her to the Women's Relief Society for assistance.

Department Order to Investigate Confiscated Copper Coins: The case of a large amount of copper coins confiscated by the Public Security First Branch Bureau is now being directly appealed by the original plaintiff, Wei Dun, to the Ministry of Finance, alleging that the Public Security Bureau has delayed judgment and penalties. The Ministry has instructed the Provincial Government to order the county to investigate and reply. Both the Ministry of Civil Affairs and the Ministry of Finance are aware that the copper coins were reported by Nie Jingdu and Bo as circulating within the county. If this is true, they should be returned. The instruction has arrived at the county, directing it to report on how the case is being handled for reference. Yesterday (the 6th), the county government, in addition to reporting the handling process to the province for forwarding to the Ministry, also submitted reports to both ministries for instructions.

Education Department Orders Investigation of Stolen Files: The Education Department, finding the circumstances of the alleged theft of files concerning County Middle School Principal Bao in the Education Bureau to be strange, has specially dispatched Provincial Inspector Cao Shutian to Yangzhou on the 6th to join the county in investigating the truth of how the files, as well as various case files and account books, were stolen from the Education Bureau, so as to report to the department for verification and action.

Jingjiang

Ministry of Civil Affairs Dispatches Investigator: The Ministry of Civil Affairs has dispatched Zhu Hejun to Jingjiang to thoroughly investigate the conflict between County Magistrate Wang and Examiner Yin Cheng, and to conduct a particularly detailed investigation into the salt tax fine and the release of bandit monk Ming Kun, Wang Yinzhen, and illegal salt merchant Li Wangshi. This has now been completed, and Zhu Hejun has left Jingjiang.

Brutal Robbery and Murder on Saltwater Boat Case Solved: Wang Sanyou of Taixing owns two boats specializing in the saltwater business. On June 16th of this year, he transported a boatload of saltwater to Taixing for sale, while his wife lived on another boat. On the way, the boat encountered bandits. The boat owner and his crew were killed by the bandits, and the boat was robbed. His wife waited in Jingjiang for many days without any news. After repeated investigations, some said that he had already been killed by bandits, but the truth could not be determined. Unexpectedly, yesterday (the 6th), her husband's boat was seen coming from the north. Wang's wife, without making a sound, immediately reported to the Security Corps, which dispatched corps members to arrest a total of eight people, including Ye Zixing, Qian Rongchu, Sun Di, Qian Jiulin, Wang Yunzhang, Wu Zhiming, Zhu Jiaoshi, and Bao Renyi. They were handed over to the county government for interrogation.

Jiaxing

Policeman Sentenced for Stealing Watch: Pan Fuqing, a policeman from the Jiaxing County Public Security Bureau, stole a silver watch from traveler Sima Fengjiu at the Shaoxing Hotel on Dongma Road while inspecting travelers at various hotels late last month. After Public Security Bureau Chief Shen Weihan discovered this, Pan was dismissed and sent to the local court for interrogation. Yesterday, Pan Fuqing was sentenced to eight months in prison for robbery.

County Magistrate Sworn In and Bureau Chief Takes Office: Jiaxing County Magistrate Shi Nong took over office on the 19th of last month. The swearing-in ceremony was held on the 8th to formally take office. In addition, Construction Bureau Chief Zhang Shiqing was transferred to Hangzhou County by order of the department. Liang Hua was appointed to fill the vacancy. It is reported that Bureau Chief Liang has already taken over office yesterday.

Hangzhou

Ministry of Finance Raising Back Pay Expenses: The Ministry of Finance previously stated that the provincial treasury was extremely depleted, and the expenses for the 18th fiscal year (June) of various agencies had not yet been fully disbursed, accumulating to over 200,000. The province is now planning to expedite the final accounts and is issuing funds as the various bureaus submit their payments. If this is insufficient, a small temporary loan will be negotiated to clear the accounts within one month.

Dispute Resolved in Ministry-Province Telephone Line: The dispute over the Ministry-Province telephone line has lasted more than half a year. Now, after Commissioner Cheng's efforts to mediate, both parties resumed connections yesterday (the 8th). From now on, users in Shanghai and Hangzhou can talk immediately. The Ministry and Bureau have also notified all locations that those directly calling from Hangzhou to Shanghai must first register with the Ministry and Bureau. The fee for calling from Shanghai to various counties in Zhejiang Province will be calculated according to the provincial bureau's regulations.

Ningbo

Zhu Peide and Others Go to Fenghua to Meet Commander-in-Chief Chiang: Zhu Peide, Dong Xianguang, Central Alternate Committee Member Miao Peicheng, and others came to Ningbo from Shanghai yesterday morning to go to Fenghua to meet Chiang. After arriving at Xikou and learning that Chairman Chiang was at Miaogao Platform, they transferred to Miaogao Platform to meet him and report on matters. They had lunch at Miaogao Platform and returned to Xikou at 4:00 PM, lodging at Wuling Elementary School in the evening. It is said that after official business is completed today, they will take a boat back to Shanghai and then to Nanjing.

Police Rob Golden Bracelet: On the Yin-Fenghua automobile road at the Fenghua station at 5:00 PM, a woman in her twenties, carrying two children and several pieces of luggage, including clothes, a gold bracelet on her right hand, and a gold watch on her left hand, planned to take a car to Ningbo. A police officer at the station, seeing that the woman's gold bracelet was worth more than a hundred yuan, suddenly had the idea to steal it. When the woman took the two children onto the car and returned to the station to get her luggage, the officer immediately robbed her. A road worker held the woman back. The woman cried out loudly, but the car drove away. The station chief entered his office, closed the door, and pretended not to hear. After the police officer obtained the bracelet, he abandoned his post and fled. Afterward, the woman reported the incident to the local Public Security Bureau, which dispatched police to arrest the road worker and bring the station chief to the bureau for questioning. Police were also dispatched in all directions to apprehend the thief.

Theft and Robbery of Wealthy Merchant in Xiachen, Fenghua: At 10:00 PM the night before last, more than ten bandits suddenly came to the home of Qiu Wenqing, a wealthy merchant in Xiachen, Fenghua, and broke down the door. Two bandits stood guard at the door, while the rest entered to rob. Qiu had prepared in advance and hid all the valuables in his home elsewhere. He was also not at home that night. Only several dozen yuan in silver dollars, more than a hundred corner in small money, and more than thirty pieces of ordinary clothing were stolen, totaling a loss of no more than a hundred yuan.

Chiang Jianren to Be Sent to Japan for Investigation: Chiang Jianren, head of the Second Propaganda Brigade of the General Headquarters, is only twenty-six years old and was formerly the director of the Political Training Office of the Sixth Division of the National Army and the director of the Social Bureau of the Special Municipality of Hankou, as well as a member of the Reorganization Committee and director of Training of the Hankou Special Municipal Party Headquarters. During the recent central government's campaign against Yan and Feng, Chiang served as the head of the Second Propaganda Brigade of the General Headquarters, making significant contributions. Chiang came to Ningbo a few days ago to go to Fenghua to meet with the Commander-in-Chief and report on important matters. Yesterday, he took a boat to Shanghai and then to Nanjing to handle the closing of the Propaganda Brigade. It is also said that Chiang was instructed by the Commander-in-Chief to go to Japan after the Propaganda Brigade was closed to investigate the political, economic, and social situation. He will be setting sail overseas soon.

Shangyu

Fierce Mother-in-Law Twice Divorces Daughter-in-Law: The wife of the late Yin Sheng, a native of Wufuzhen in the Northern Village of Shangyu, is known for her fierceness. She has two sons, the elder named Zhenglin and the younger Zhilin, both of whom are merchants in Shanghai. In 1927, the elder daughter-in-law, Xu, was divorced by order due to the mother-in-law's dissatisfaction. Resentful, Xu became a nun. At the time, the villagers disapproved of her behavior. Unexpectedly, Yin's wife did not repent and recently developed resentment towards her younger daughter-in-law, Liu, resorting to whipping and slander. Unable to bear the pain, Liu attempted suicide by taking Teng Huang poison but was rescued. Afterward, the mother-in-law again forced her daughter-in-law to return to her maiden home. When the younger son in Shanghai heard the news, he rushed back. Knowing his mother's stubborn nature, he did not dare to dissuade her. It is now learned that Liu's family has requested the mediation of Du Xisheng and Li Jiantang of Yiting, but to no avail. They have officially requested assistance from the Women's Association.

Letter

Letter from Wang Kechang, District Chief of the Ninth District of Qingpu

Recently, I read a news item in your newspaper's local correspondence column on October 25th, titled "Illegal Salt Merchant He Duo," which is inconsistent with the facts. On the afternoon of that day at around 2:00 PM, volunteer members of the Security Corps noticed a local ruffian, Luo A'jin, arguing with someone with an unknown surname over a package. They intervened, but the person with the unknown surname took the opportunity to escape. They only brought Luo A'jin and a package to my department (not the district office). When I returned to the town from Qingpu (to deliver silver), I inquired about the matter and immediately opened the package in public. There were only five pieces of clothing and nothing else. Therefore, it was sent to the Public Security Fourth Sub-station for investigation. The details in your newspaper are completely inconsistent with the facts. I am writing this special letter to request a correction. Wang Kechang, District Chief of the Ninth District of Qingpu County.

Education News Highlights

Ministry of Education Orders Three Weeks of National Calendar New Year Holiday

No Winter Vacation Allowed

Nanjing, 8th - The Ministry of Education has ordered all provincial education departments and all public and private schools to uniformly observe a three-week National Calendar New Year holiday from the 19th year onward, with the exception of Guangdong Province, which, due to its proximity to the tropics, is allowed to reduce the New Year holiday by one week and add it to the summer vacation, following the revised regulations on the school year, academic schedule, and holiday dates. No winter vacation is allowed in addition to the National Calendar New Year holiday.

Ministry of Education Orders No Permission to Confer

Honorary Degrees

Before the Degree Law is Promulgated

Nanjing, 8th - The Ministry of Education has ordered all provincial education departments not to confer honorary degrees without authorization before the Degree Law is promulgated.

Wu Zhihui

Discusses the Turmoil at National Central University

The Ministry of Education is Responsible for Mismanagement

Zhang Naiyan Should Have Resigned Earlier

Released After Chairman Chiang Returns to Nanjing

Nanjing, 8th - Before the establishment of the Ministry of Education in 1928, the University Council hired Wu Zhihui as the president of National Central University. Wu did not accept the position, and the University Council ordered Zhang Naiyan to serve as acting president until Wu arrived at the university. This matter is known to the education community. Because of Wu's relationship with National Central University and his status as a veteran of the Party-State and the education community, the reporter specifically visited Wu at the Reception Center of the Construction Committee on the afternoon of the 8th to inquire about his views on the campus unrest. According to Wu, he has not heard about the affairs of National Central University recently and has no opinions to express. In general, schools cannot be run if politics are not on track. Student involvement in school administration has become a common practice since the May Fourth Movement. National Central University and the Ministry of Education are very close, and monthly reports are submitted to the ministry, such as exceeding the administrative expenses quota or improper school administrative organization. The Ministry of Education has the direct authority to correct these matters. Because of the Ministry of Education's dereliction of duty, the students have risen up to demand the improvement of school affairs. It is the students' duty to study at school. What does it matter if the president has hobbies or not? The president is like the local temple in the village. What does the temple's decline have to do with the villagers? I have repeatedly advised Mr. Zhang to resign as president earlier. Recently, seeing the worsening environment, Zhang's intention to resign has become stronger. Chairman Chiang has a plan to completely reorganize National Central University because of the complexity of the internal elements of National Central University. This plan has been very clearly expressed in his conversation with reporters. After Chairman Chiang returns to Nanjing, he can release the plan and the president can implement it in accordance with the reorganization plan. The reporter also asked about the mutual debate between Zhang Naiyan and Jiang Menglin. Wu said that this matter is a misunderstanding on both sides. Once it is explained, there will be no prejudice.

Suzhou-Zhenjiang Principals' Meeting

Clear Payment of Nine-Ten Months of Back Pay Within November

Submit a Petition to the Education Department for the Speedy Promulgation of Protection for Education Personnel

Request an Explanation of the Meaning of Using the Word "Dispatch" for Appointing Principals

(Zhenjiang Correspondence) The Jiangsu Provincial Secondary Education Research Association (formerly the Provincial Secondary School Principals' Joint Association) held a meeting yesterday at Zhenjiang Middle School. Attendees included Xiao Mingqin, Zhou Xingbo, Chen Gugin, Chen Jingzhi, Lu Shu, (Zhu Dingjun representing), Shao Bosheng, Peng Binghou, Wang Xiacai, Gu Zhongqi, Zhu Lu, Wang Maozu, Ren Zhongmin, Xue Qiaodong (Ren representing), Zhang Jingqiu, Zhang Haicheng, Jiang Xuezhu, Tao Xuan, Zhu Guangyu, (Attached representing), Sun Shenhuang, (Zhang representing), Han Yanmen, (Zhang representing), Feng Limin, Zheng Xigu, Liao Jianan (Zheng representing). The resolutions are recorded as follows:

(1) Submit a petition to the Education Department to clear the payment of nine-ten months of back pay within November. (2) Re-submit the case of Principal Xiao's humiliation at Suzhou Middle School, urging the provincial government to investigate and handle it impartially. (3) Submit a request to expedite the disbursement of temporary funds for the 18th year in order to repay debts and prepare final accounts. (4) After the revenue from the student dormitories in the 19th year is included in the general budget, if the school's routine and temporary expenses are insufficient, a petition should be submitted to the Education Department to thoroughly investigate the actual needs of each school, determine measures to remedy the insufficient funding, and stipulate the temporary expenses for each school in order to carry out projects. (5) The academic qualifications issued by the Ministry this year have many obstacles that require flexible solutions. (6) Submit a petition to the Education Department to forward to the Ministry of Education for the speedy promulgation of protection for education personnel. (7) Submit a petition to the Ministry of Education to explain the meaning of using the word "dispatch" instead of "select and appoint" regarding the selection and appointment of primary and secondary school principals. (8) Organize and publish the resolutions of previous conferences that have not been implemented for joint study, discussion, and implementation methods. (9) Submit a petition to the Education Department to request the Finance Committee to find ways to increase revenue. (10) The tuition fees collected by each school will be summarized at the end of the 19th year and temporarily not reported.

More than ten student representatives acknowledged and signed the agreement. The Waseda University disturbance, which lasted for twenty-two days, has been resolved satisfactorily.

Elementary Education Textbook

Standards Compilation Committee Regulations

The Ministry of Education Announces Twelve Articles

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education announced the regulations for the Primary Education Textbook Compilation Standards Formulation Committee. The regulations are recorded as follows:

Ministry of Education Primary Education Textbook Compilation Standards Formulation Committee Regulations

(Article 1) The Ministry of Education establishes the Ministry of Education Primary Education Textbook Compilation Standards Formulation Committee (hereinafter referred to as "the Committee") to improve kindergarten and elementary school textbooks and formulate standards for compiling such books. (Article 2) The tasks of the Primary Education Textbook Compilation Standards Formulation Committee are as follows: 1. Study the advantages and disadvantages of kindergarten and elementary school textbooks. 2. Investigate the opinions of kindergarten and elementary school teachers on the textbooks they use and the actual results of their teaching. 3. Organize and study the results of the investigation and design improvement methods. 4. Draft and revise the textbook compilation standards for elementary schools and kindergartens. (Article 3) The members of the Committee are appointed by the Minister of Education, including the Director of the General Education Department, the Director of the Compilation and Review Department, one Counselor, one Section Chief of the General Education Department, several staff members, and several compilers. The following personnel are also invited to serve: A. Three primary education experts. B. Three to five current elementary school principals and kindergarten and elementary school educators. C. Three to five people with experience in editing textbooks. (Article 4) The Committee has five standing committee members appointed by the Minister of Education from among the members who are Ministry of Education staff, with one member serving as the chairman. (Article 5) The Committee may invite the Minister and Vice-Minister of Education to attend meetings and express their opinions. (Article 6) The Committee may entrust education experts and teachers who teach in the field to assist in subject-specific research. (Article 7) The members of the Committee are unpaid, but those who do not reside in Beijing may receive travel expenses to attend meetings. (Article 8) Important matters resolved by the Committee must be approved and implemented by the Minister of Education. (Article 9) The compilation standards formulated by the Committee shall be approved and promulgated by the Minister of Education. (Article 10) The Committee has two secretaries responsible for recording, communication, and other matters, appointed concurrently by the Minister of Education from among the Ministry of Education staff. (Article 11) These regulations shall be implemented upon approval by the Minister of Education. (Article 12) These regulations may be amended by the resolution of the Committee and the consent of the Minister of Education.

Minutes of the Jiangsu Literacy Movement Propaganda Committee

The second meeting of the Jiangsu Provincial Literacy Movement Propaganda Committee was held at the Education Department at 2:00 PM on the 6th. Committee members present were Zhang Ji, Zhou (representative of the Agriculture and Mining Department), Zhang Xiangwei (representative of the Ministry of Civil Affairs), Gao Yang, Qi Xiyong (representatives of provincial social education institutions), Lan Weibin, Ling Shaozu, Xiao (representatives of the provincial party headquarters), Yu Qingtang (Third Section Chief of the Education Department), and Chen Hexian (Director of the Education Department). Secretary Liu Shaozhen was present, and Chen Hexian chaired the meeting. Liu Shaozhen recorded the minutes. The meeting began at 2:00 PM with the chairman respectfully reading the Premier's will. (Reporting Matters) (1) The provincial government sent a seal to the association with the words "Seal of the Jiangsu Provincial Literacy Movement Propaganda Committee," which was announced for use on October 29th. (2) The Secretariat of the Provincial Government replied that all external documents of the association should be in the form of a letter. (3) The Secretariat of the Provincial Government replied that the association's detailed rules for operation had been approved by the chairman, but the word "assistant" in "assistant clerk" should be deleted, and the word "(report)" in Article 16 should be changed to "(letter)." (4) The Provincial Party Reorganization Committee, the Secretariat of the Provincial Government, the Ministry of Civil Affairs, the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining, the Zhenjiang Provincial Mass Education Center, and the Nanjing Provincial Mass Education Center have successively replied, appointing special clerks to the association. (5) The Education Department has replied, appointing permanent clerks and clerks to each group of the association. (6) The Literacy Movement Committee of Tongshan County has telegraphed to inform about the launch of the literacy movement. (Discussion Matters) (1) The draft program for the progress of the literacy movement in the province has now been reviewed, revised, and submitted for consideration and approval. Resolution: The draft was revised, approved, and submitted to the provincial government for approval and implementation. (2) The draft budget for the association's expenses was prepared and submitted for consideration and approval. Resolution: It was decided that the annual recurring expenses would be 4,500 yuan, and the special expenses for the propaganda week would be 2,000 yuan each year. The association will prepare a budget and submit it to the provincial government for approval. (3) Regarding the assignment of duty clerks to groups, the resolution was as follows: General Affairs Group: He Xuyou, Xu Yanfan; Propaganda Group: Geng Tonglin, Hua Shu; Investigation Group: Chen Tianyu, Zhang Xiangwei; Design Group: Liu Xiangxiao, Zhao Guangtao. (4) Regarding the appointment of the association's staff, the resolution was as follows: The association will send a letter of appointment.

Local News

Director Xu of the Municipal Education Bureau Speaks on

The Misguided Establishment of an Education Department by the Municipal Council

Director Xu Peihuang of the Municipal Education Bureau spoke to a reporter from the Education Society about the establishment of an Education Department by the Municipal Council of the Public Concession as follows: Since the establishment of the Municipal Government in 1927, all educational administration in the city has been handled by this bureau. Over the years, the Municipal Government has paid great attention to education throughout the city. The annual budget accounts for about 20% of the city's revenue, and no effort has been spared in reorganizing private schools. However, the two concessions in the city, relying on unequal treaties as a talisman, lie across the city, causing difficulties for the city's educational administration from time to time. It is found that the revenue in the concessions is four or five times higher than that in the Chinese area, and the burden on Chinese people is particularly heavy, but the concession authorities have always not paid attention to Chinese education. The curricula of most of the primary and secondary schools are biased towards English and do not follow the regulations set by the Ministry. Recently, they have even presumptuously established a Chinese Education Department, which is really strange. If they claim to be intending to rectify education, then this is not their share of responsibilities. If they claim to be deliberately sabotaging education, then this is even more impermissible. Regardless of their intentions, even in terms of its naming, the Education Department is the name of the highest educational institution in our country. The Municipal Council is only a private organization of foreigners in China, and should give extra respect to the highest political authority in the locality. It should not presumptuously steal the name and confuse the order. Anything heard is difficult for any citizen to tolerate, let alone this bureau, which is responsible for the city's education. I dare not be silent and report it to the Municipal Government and the Ministry of Education. In addition to reporting to the Municipal Government and the Ministry of Education, I have especially summarized the facts to inform the people of the country that all educational undertakings in the concessions should be handled in accordance with the regulations set by the Ministry, and no one else is allowed to overstep their authority. Moreover, they dare to privately establish a name that insinuates our country's ministries. The Municipal Council is really hard to blame, and so on.

Letter from Eight Elementary Schools in Ningxiang to Foreign Minister Wang

Regarding the Recovery of Educational Rights

A letter from teachers and staff of the Eighth Elementary School of the Ningbo Compatriot Association to Foreign Minister Wang states: "Wang Minister, Foreign Minister of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing, I respectfully inform you that recently, the Municipal Council of the Shanghai Public Concession, under the name of the Education Department of the Municipal Council, distributed school survey forms to the schools in the concession, requesting that they be sent. It is urgently trying to interfere with the education in the concession and disrupt the unified system of education in our country. We, the members of the school, deeply regret that the concessions are bound by unequal treaties, causing the administration to fall into the hands of others, and we, the people, are trapped in deep water and fire and have suffered all kinds of pain. However, apart from running a few schools, the authorities have not interfered with the public and private schools of our Chinese people. Now that your department is working hard to recover the concessions and the Municipal Government is advocating to take over the educational rights of the concessions, the authorities are wantonly and recklessly trying to seize educational power and are even using the name of the highest educational institution in our country for their department, openly insulting our country. This fully proves that the ambition of imperialists to invade our country has only increased. The policy of our late Premier to recover the concessions and abolish unequal treaties has not been implemented yet. In front of last month, we submitted a report to the Municipal Government requesting serious negotiations, and the newspapers sent letters to all walks of life, unanimously advocating. Although the voices are small, they are related to the future of the Party and the country and are by no means small matters. Therefore, as soon as this letter was sent, all walks of life responded one after another and took further steps to carry out the movement to take over the educational rights of the concessions. Judging from the excitement of the people's minds as recorded in the recent newspapers, one can get a general idea. However, the Municipal Government has not yet made any statement. Your seat is concerned about the Party and the country and is in charge of negotiations. I implore you to follow the Premier's will and carefully plan a method to deal with the situation and strive to carry out the proposition with the spirit of revolution. Also, order the Municipal Government to immediately propose negotiations, the hearts of the people will not die, how can a weak country have no diplomacy? Justice is present, and the powerful will eventually submit. I respectfully admire your prestige and look forward to your reply. I miss the Party and the country and feel extremely cold. I must send a telegram and cannot wait any longer. I respectfully await your orders. Respectfully submitted by Zhang Li, Liu Canfang, Liu Youshu, Shi Maotang, Cao Shijie, and Zhang Yunying, currently teachers and staff of the Eighth Elementary School of the Ningbo Association in Shanghai, bowing in respect."

Famous Figures in the Education Community

Organizing a Phonetic Symbols Promotion Association

Cai Yuanpei, Wu Jingheng, Liu Zhan'en, Ou Yuan, Chen Heqin, He Bingsong, and others have initiated the organization of a Phonetic Symbols Promotion Association to promote the application of phonetic symbols. Their declaration and brief regulations are recorded as follows: (Declaration) In 1913, the Ministry of Education held a conference on the unification of pronunciation and produced forty phonetic symbols to make it easier for illiterate people to recognize characters and for literate people to unify pronunciation. Since then, the education community has continuously carried out the movement to unify the national language. However, for more than ten years, the intellectual class has not yet achieved the hope of unification, and the literacy of the masses has not been affected at all. This year's National Education Conference knows that popularizing literacy is more important than other issues, so it changed the name of phonetic letters to phonetic symbols and prepared to add phonetic symbols next to Chinese characters everywhere as a tool for popularizing education, which in effect will also broadcast most of the national language phonemes to the people, and can also get a lot of help in unifying the national language. Now the education authorities have orders to promote it, and the society and the masses should also have an expression of promotion. Therefore, we unite with comrades to organize this association, hoping that all circles will join in helping and guiding. We hereby declare. "Brief Regulations" (1) Name: The name of this association is the Phonetic Symbols Promotion Association. (2) Purpose: The purpose of the association is to study and promote phonetic symbols. (3) Membership: Anyone who approves of the purpose of the association and is introduced by two or more members may become a member of the association. (4) Staff: 1. The association has nine executive committee members to form an executive committee to preside over all association affairs. 2. The executive committee has three standing committee members. 3. The executive committee may hire several clerks as it deems appropriate to assist with association affairs. (5) Supplementary Rules: If these brief regulations are not perfect, they may be amended by a public resolution of the members. It is said that the preparatory office of the association is temporarily located in the Youth Association on Sichuan Road.

Notice from the Board of Directors: The board of directors of China Public School posted a notice at the school on the 6th of this month, stating: "Two years ago, all the students of our school sent telegrams and representatives to urge Principal Yu Youren to come, but he could not. This time, the board of directors elected him, and after our representatives repeatedly urged him and all the faculty and students repeatedly welcomed him, he finally agreed to come to the school on the 10th of this month. He is coming despite his illness, and his enthusiasm for maintaining our school is truly something we are extremely grateful for. He has been a volunteer director of our school for more than 20 years, an old teacher of our school for 20 years, the most powerful founder of our school, and the drafter of the declaration for founding our school. His relationship with our school is closer than anyone else's. He is an old poet of our time and a senior figure in the educational and journalistic circles. Many thoughtful middle-aged and young people have been influenced or trained by him. His indomitable spirit will surely invigorate the whole school and enable our school to achieve the greatest development in the shortest possible time. This is what we firmly believe. We anticipate the development within our school and wish Principal Yu good health." The Vocational Education Society's Eighth Academic Lecture

The China Vocational Education Society held its eighth academic lecture yesterday, inviting Huang Renzhi as the lecturer. He began speaking at 4:15 PM. Although it was raining heavily at the time, many people enthusiastically participated. Chairman Yang Weiyu introduced the lecturer, and Mr. Huang spoke on the topic of "Philosophy of Life," which was roughly divided into the following points: (1) Man and Heaven and Earth; (2) Man and Things; (3) Harmony with Things; (4) The Views of Life Advocated by Past Philosophers; (5) The Views of Life Held by Ordinary People Today; (6) The Views of Life We Believe Are Appropriate. The sixth point also included the following items: 1. Based on a global perspective; 2. Maximize empathy for people and things; 3. Peaceful attitude; 4. Spirit of vigorous progress; 5. Scientific methods; 6. Socialized organization; 7. Efforts based on one's position; 8. Strive to maximize benefits for others and minimize benefits for oneself; 9. Strive to maximize happiness for the majority and minimize sacrifices for the minority; 10. Be willing to sacrifice all one's happiness if necessary; 11. Strive for success with utmost effort, but have no regrets if one fails.

Huadong Basketball Team Defeats Mailings Yesterday

Score: 34 to 14

The Huadong Sports Company's basketball team played a friendly match against Mailings last night at 8 PM at the West YMCA. The Mailings team has undergone major changes, with many of its former star players having scattered. Only Wei Shipi remains. Their performance is far from what it used to be. It is hoped that after three or four weeks of rigorous training, they can regain their former glory. The Huadong team, on the other hand, is made up of top talents of the time, and it was always expected that they would stand out. What the team needs most now is strategy and internal and external cooperation. The match was divided into four quarters, each lasting ten minutes. In the first and fourth quarters, both sides fielded their best players, which was quite impressive. The rest of the time, they were like a sheet of loose sand. Huadong's initial lineup consisted of Liang Guo, Fu Wufan, Li Chengyuan, Wang Jinpeng, and Lu Zhensui. Liang opened the scoring for Huadong when a pass from Li was grabbed by Liang and thrown into the basket. Mailings veteran Wei Shipi scored a basket, tying the score. Li Chengyuan then took advantage of free throw opportunities, scoring one himself and having Liang score another, quickly giving Huadong a 5-2 lead. Soon after, Fu scored, and Li and Liang also scored, while Mailings, under the close watch of Lu and Wang, only had Bi Shaopo score a basket. The result of the first quarter was Huadong 11 points, Mailings 4 points. The lineup was greatly changed in the second quarter, and Mailings' momentum increased. At the end of the first half, Huadong had 13 points and Mailings had 10 points. The lineup was changed again in the second half, and Huadong continued to take the lead and was very active. The score in the third quarter was Huadong 17, Mailings 12. In the fourth quarter, the two teams again fielded their best players to make a final push. Although Huadong benefited from their great momentum and won the match, there was no outstanding performance in terms of team cooperation and strategy. This may be because the team has not been formed for long. The final score was 31-14, with Huadong winning. The referee was Beilisi.

Chizhi Basketball Team Defeats Qingguang

Score: 46 to 33

The Chizhi and Qingguang basketball teams played a friendly match last night at 7:30 PM at the China Basketball Room. The competition between the two sides was very fierce. Chizhi had average talent and great courage, and they fought hard throughout the match. Qingguang relied entirely on the command of Tan Dahua, and although the rest of the players worked hard, they found it difficult to penetrate under the close watch of the opponents. Chizhi took the lead all the way and remained in a leading position. As a result, Chizhi won 46-33. At the beginning of the match, Chizhi launched a strong attack and scored several points in a row, leading by scores such as 6-0 and 12-3. Qingguang worked hard to catch up and made some progress. The score at halftime was 18-14, with Chizhi winning. In the second half, Qingguang launched a counterattack and made some progress, once reaching a score of 19-20, with only one point separating the two teams. However, after that, Chizhi's momentum became very strong, and Yang Linyu, Wei Haiqing, and Liu Peichu scored repeatedly, quickly increasing the score to 40-23. After that, Chizhi's defense relaxed slightly, and Qingguang took the opportunity to attack and catch up with several points. As a result, Chizhi finally won 46-33.
