Shen Bao Special Issue on the National Industrial and Commercial Conference, No. 9

Eighth Day of the Industrial and Commercial Conference

Closed Yesterday, Issued a Declaration

Resolved to Organize an International Trade Association, The Public Works Department Appoints Preparatory Personnel, Issued a Circular Telegram Requesting the Return of Detained Vehicles and That No Further Detentions Occur

Commentary

Industrial and Commercial Policies by Zhang Yi'ou

Industry and commerce are the crystallization of opportune timing, geographical advantages, and human harmony. In other words, the three—timing, geographical advantages, and policies—are indispensable. Policy is especially important. With good policies, even if timing and geographical advantages are somewhat lacking, it is not difficult to make up for them as much as possible. Without good policies, even if timing and geographical advantages are superior, they cannot be fully utilized. Our country is vast in territory and rich in resources, and its people are diligent, simple, and hard-working. It can be established as a nation based on agriculture, and it can also be established as a nation based on industry and commerce. Good opportunities often arise. A brief examination reveals that there is generally an excellent opportunity every ten years:

(1) In 1895, the Treaty of Shimonoseki allowed foreigners to establish factories in China, giving us the opportunity to imitate them nearby. Although this had more disadvantages than advantages, most of our existing industries and businesses have been formed by such observation and imitation, which must be regarded as a kind of opportunity.

(2) In 1906, the United States banned Chinese laborers, and we boycotted American goods, giving us the opportunity to resolutely promote national goods, which was a relatively advantageous situation. Subsequently, the May Fourth Movement in 1919 and the May Thirtieth Incident in 1925 led to an increase in domestic production each time the banner of boycotting foreign goods was raised. Tracing back to the source, it is necessary to give credit to the first determination in 1905.

(3) The period of the European War from 1914 to 1919 provided us with an opportunity for full development. It was a truly unexpected good opportunity. If, at that time, our country's various basic industries had already reached a considerable scale, and we were able to expand our own machinery and chemical materials as much as possible, and to expand our shipping and international exchange, it would not have been difficult to turn poverty into wealth, to leap from an agricultural country to an industrial and commercial country, to leap from a silver standard to a gold standard, and to leap from a debtor to a creditor. Even if the foundation laid by predecessors was flawed, if we could unite from top to bottom and advance at double speed, we could at least increase mass production and transform the long-standing excess of imports into an excess of exports. Unexpectedly, the military and political authorities began to actively engage in internal disputes at this time, completely wiping out this unprecedented opportunity without realizing it. Impatience in small matters ruins great plans, and it can only be attributed to fate.

(4) In 1927, the sixteenth year of the Republic, the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, and the following year, it recovered Peiping, unifying the country. Dr. Sun Yat-sen's "The International Development of China" became popular throughout the country, providing a compass for opening up new things and completing tasks for future generations, representing the newest and greatest opportunity. Everyone missed the opportunity of the European War, but Dr. Sun Yat-sen uniquely conceived and planned this grand strategy. "The International Development of China" was completed shortly after the end of the European War, truly embodying the idea that "deep sorrow inspires wisdom." From now on, we do not need to talk excessively about policy, nor is it possible to formulate new policies. We can only sincerely and wholeheartedly accept Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings.

In summary, Dr. Sun Yat-sen's plan takes the development of transportation and the construction of ports as its warp, and the establishment of large factories and the revitalization of industry as its weft, encompassing all aspects of trade promotion and benefiting workers. We may not be able to fully grasp its essence in our lifetime, but with our limited knowledge, we can glimpse its great characteristics, which can be roughly summarized into two points:

(1) The "industry" in "The International Development of China" is based on the Principle of People's Livelihood, not capitalism. Therefore, important enterprises should focus on state-owned operations in order to universally realize the Principle of People's Livelihood and avoid excessive development of private capital, which could lead to class struggle.

(2) The "plan" in "The International Development of China" is comprehensive and cyclical, not haphazard. Therefore, everything that should be done is considered in advance in order to avoid the drawbacks of being fragmented, incomplete, or putting the cart before the horse. However, when discussing development in detail, it is necessary to seek nourishment from the following four principles: (1) We must choose the most favorable path to attract foreign investment. (2) We must meet the most urgent needs of the people. (3) We must strive for the least resistance. (4) We must choose the most suitable location. Supposing that after the European War, the belligerent countries and even the neutral countries could sincerely assist our construction with 60 million US dollars per day or 21.9 billion US dollars per year as Dr. Sun Yat-sen hoped, not only would our country be able to make rapid progress, but the unemployment problems of various countries would also not suddenly arise (The increasing number of unemployed workers has become a universal phenomenon in various countries. The authorities have no solutions. Some advocate using these unemployed workers in construction projects, but they do not know that in countries where culture has reached a considerable level, construction projects are no more than a careful embellishment, the funds used are equivalent to being stranded, and all labor is equivalent to being wasted. It is far better to follow Dr. Sun Yat-sen's plan to directly or indirectly help us develop, invest in favorable paths, and use people in beneficial things). Unfortunately, people from various countries did not have this ambition and waited and watched, and they have not understood that a great opportunity has almost passed. Although we sincerely accept the entire plan of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the order of implementation, the scale, and the speed of success may have to be changed to some extent in reality. Take the "industry" as an example. Dr. Sun Yat-sen believed that a talented but poor young man had wealthy relatives who could help him. Therefore, he planned for him to first enter university, then study abroad and intern, and then bring back machinery when he returned to China to establish a large enterprise. However, if his relatives are snobbish and absolutely unwilling to help him succeed, then this young man can only do his best within his limited means, or work part-time and study part-time, or operate on a small scale in order to gradually achieve his goal, still living up to Dr. Sun Yat-sen's high expectations. This is what is called "acting for profit, acting for peace, or acting reluctantly, but their success is the same."

In the spring of 1928, Minister of Industry and Commerce Kong Xiangxi's administrative declaration outlined sixteen points, the main points being (taking the Principle of People's Livelihood as the goal and Dr. Sun Yat-sen's "The International Development of China" as the guide, protecting existing enterprises on the one hand, and seeking to develop new opportunities on the other, consolidating the national economy on the one hand, and increasing the welfare of workers on the other, cultivating the vitality of industry with the spirit of labor-capital cooperation, and promoting international cooperation with the principle of amicable trade, carrying out construction in order of urgency and priority). (This is a simplified version of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's plan. Our country's industrial and commercial policies already have Dr. Sun Yat-sen's "The International Development of China" in its entirety and Minister Kong's administrative declaration in its essence. Who am I? I should naturally narrate rather than create. However, based on the current situation of our country, I dare to seek even greater simplicity in the policies that Minister Kong has already simplified, so that they are easier to implement, and I will elaborate on a few points as follows:

(1) Establish a definite protection policy. In all aspects of formulating tariffs, revising commercial treaties, organizing internal taxes, and drafting laws and regulations, we must recognize the protection policy as the only savior of infant industries. Externally, we must not fear the strong, and internally, we must not hesitate to sacrifice. It is best to go all out. A committee should be formed jointly by the Ministries of Industry and Commerce, Agriculture and Mining, Finance, Railways, Communications, and Foreign Affairs to conduct joint research in order to avoid the drawback of each department formulating its own policies without being consistent.

(2) Encourage private enterprises. Dr. Sun Yat-sen advocated that state-owned enterprises should be subject to two conditions: (1) those with a monopolistic nature that cannot be entrusted to individuals, and (2) those that are difficult to operate and require a large amount of capital, and that require the use of foreign capital and foreign experts. As for those that can be entrusted to individuals or that are more suitable for private operation than state operation, he explicitly instructed us (should be done by individuals, encouraged by the state, and protected by law). He also said (If we want to facilitate the development of individual enterprises in China, the suicidal tax system that has been practiced should be abolished immediately, the chaotic currency should be improved, and all kinds of official obstacles must be removed. In particular, it is necessary to assist with convenient transportation. Now that state-owned enterprises are plagued by financial difficulties and cannot be established, Minister Kong has strongly advocated that the nine basic industries be reduced to five, but even one has not yet been established. Therefore, for private enterprises, we should naturally do our best to encourage them. In addition to rigorously implementing the existing Law on the Encouragement of Special Industries and the Special Tax Law on Machine-Made Goods, we should further expand them. Even for basic industries with low capital and high profits that should be state-owned, I believe that several types can be designated to be contracted by merchants using the guaranteed interest method, and for industries with a monopolistic nature, they should be opened up appropriately under government supervision.

(3) Concentrate strength externally and harmonize interests internally. The organization of our country's industry and commerce is generally small in scale and its strength is scattered, making it unable to compete with foreign merchants who are skilled in manipulation. Important foreign enterprises are not only united throughout the country, but even related countries are united. Our country should imitate them and act accordingly. However, if it is not done properly, it is easy to create monopolies and mergers, which may violate party principles. Therefore, while concentrating strength externally, we must harmonize interests internally and not allow the strong to bully the weak or engage in manipulative oppression. The methods for promoting benefits and preventing abuses can be implemented through industry covenants under government guidance.

(4) Strive for labor-capital harmony. Ever since the so-called labor problem arose, relying on instigation from others, it seems that labor and capital should go to extremes and fight to the death. This is a great fallacy. The relationship between people must be like two people sharing only one piece of clothing, or two men sharing only one woman. One gain must be a loss, and there is absolutely no room for activity before an irreconcilable situation can be formed. In industrially advanced countries, this situation has gradually been reached, but our country still has unlimited natural benefits that can be jointly seized by labor and capital. Due to unskilled skills and poor tools, the working ability of the labor side is far inferior to others. If it can be gradually improved to increase efficiency, wages can be increased proportionally. Due to improper planning and poor management on the capital side, money is wasted without knowing how much. If it can strive for improvement to save money, wages can also be relaxed. I once wrote an article on "The Relationship between Labor-Capital and Engineering," which explains this principle. Here, I will only add two points:

(1) The capital side must have considerable management rights. The party and government should not interfere unless there is excessive behavior. As the saying goes, "The way to govern is to remove the extremes." The right to navigate a ship must belong to the captain. If people on the same boat or people on both sides of the shore can interfere at will, danger will immediately occur.

(2) When wages increase to a considerable level, a portion should be saved to be transformed into capital. I have spent a lot of time interacting with workers both abroad and in my own country, and I have seen that foreign workers spend their money on alcohol, while Chinese workers spend their money on gambling. Increasing wages and improving living standards are two different things. If a fixed percentage can be deducted and saved at any time to join the share capital, it can not only cultivate a habit of thrift, but also gradually bring the relationship between the labor and capital classes closer and closer together. When the Ministry of Industry and Commerce drafted the Company Law, I had this proposal, but unfortunately it was not implemented.

(5) Protect handicrafts in all cases. "Unemployment" is a term used exclusively by industrially advanced countries. "Unemployed" refers to those who have already established a career and suddenly lost it. In our country, the majority of people have never established a career or had a career. They are directly "unemployed." Not only is it difficult to start machine industries suddenly in poor and remote areas, so it is necessary to protect handicrafts to maintain livelihoods, but even in major cities, there is still a surplus of people, and those who seek manual labor in factories but cannot find it still rely on handicrafts for subsistence. In Eastern and Western countries, the number of unemployed people is only several tens of thousands at the least, and no more than several hundreds of thousands or one million at the most, which is already considered a very big problem. The number of unemployed people in our country is at least more than 100 million. How can it not be a problem? In addition to exempting native cloth from taxes, I believe that the treatment of handicrafts should at least be equal to that of machine-made foreign goods in order to be in line with the national conditions and the times.

There are also two things that can be appended here as concluding remarks:

(1) The recent import of "rationalization," in my opinion, can be said to be a good medicine for saving the times in a country where industry is still in its infancy and people are suffering from unemployment, but in a country where industry is already excessive and people are suffering from unemployment, it is no different from adding fuel to the fire. The so-called "rationalization," although its arguments are lofty and its logic is meticulous, its results are nothing more than saving labor, saving materials, saving turnover, and saving middlemen. After saving again and again, directly and indirectly, the ultimate saving is only people. Therefore, in a country that is still in its infancy, if rationalization can be used to eliminate waste, then the goods will be of good quality and low price, which can resist imports externally and guide enterprises internally. Unemployed people can also have jobs, and both industries and people will have plenty of room to maneuver. However, it is not appropriate to hold this high-sounding argument to bind all small industries or handicrafts that are temporarily difficult to rationalize due to environmental reasons, and to despise and treat them badly. In countries where industrial development is already excessive, the more rationalization there is, the more unbearable it will be. Those capitalists only know that saving labor, saving materials, saving turnover, and saving middlemen can reduce costs and lower prices in order to sell their surplus goods, but they do not know that the market is ultimately limited, and the number of unemployed people will inevitably increase even more. This is what is called knowing one thing but not knowing the other. There are no unchanging theories in the world, and there are no indestructible systems. The current industrial system has already reached the point of collapse, and the theories will also change accordingly. The industrial revolution in the future must adopt the principle of "everyone having food to eat." Proper rationalization should conform to the following principles:

(1) All arduous and demeaning work that cannot be overcome by human power or that is inhumane should be done by machines, and they must be constantly refined so that workers who operate machines are not affected by arduous and demeaning work.

(2) For all simple and noble work that can be overcome by human power and that can be done without hindering humanity, the use of machines and the degree of rationalization should be moderate so that everyone has work to do. Otherwise, if rationalization is taken to the extreme, one industry will only need one factory, and one city will only need one store. If the private property system is still implemented, it will be a case of a few being full while the majority are hungry. If the public property system is used instead, it will be a case of a few being working while the majority are at ease. In essence, it seems that neither can form a world or a life. Gandhi not only wears coarse cloth, but also carries an old-fashioned spinning machine to spin yarn. If we do not think he is crazy, then his thoughts and actions are worth studying. Moreover, in our country, the machine industry has not yet developed. In poor and remote areas, only handicrafts can accumulate small gains into large profits. How can we despise them?

(2) Regarding the recent gold price and silver devaluation turmoil, people in the field have racked their brains to address the root cause and treat the symptoms, and various opinions have been put forward in a mixed manner, but no conclusion has been reached, and it still awaits the convening of an economic conference to solicit public opinion from the whole country. I am well aware that this matter is of great importance, and a slight deviation can lead to a loss of a thousand miles. The rise and fall of a country can be determined by a single word, so I have never dared to lightly express my opinion. However, the following two points are beneficial and harmless, so I will briefly describe them:

(1) Abolish the tael and establish the yuan, and standardize auxiliary coins to use the decimal system uniformly. This is what Dr. Sun Yat-sen called "the chaotic currency system must be improved." Without doing this, it cannot become a national currency, nor can it become a country. Even without a gold rush, it should be done. After the tael is abolished and the yuan is established, it will be easier to crack down on the entry and exit of raw silver, which will also help to alleviate the gold rush.

(2) Increase production as much as possible. Eliminate warlords and bandits, and encourage both machine-made goods and handicrafts in order to drastically increase exports and sharply reduce imports. Whether it is gold coins or silver coins, they originally had a legal price in the country and were originally chips. Only when they flowed out to foreign countries were they regarded as goods and did issues of prices arise. If our country's foreign trade is in surplus rather than deficit, even if silver depreciates daily, there is no need to rush to exchange it for gold, so how can there be such panic? As for switching to the gold standard,

Seventh General Meeting

Zheng Hongnian, Chairman

The National Industry and Commerce Conference opened on the 1st. The more than 500 proposals were first divided into six groups for review. Each group was further divided into several small teams for careful review. After the proposals were deliberated one by one by the General Meeting, the important cases, such as the organization of the Industrial and Commercial Rationalization Research Association, the Labor-Capital Coordination Plan, the promotion of national goods, the change of the third accounting period, the reorganization of the tax system, and basic industries... were all approved. Some were handed over to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for promulgation and implementation, and some were handed over to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for adoption or to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for submission to the central government for implementation. After six general meetings, all cases were deliberated separately. At 9:00 a.m. on the 8th, the General Meeting Declaration was passed in the auditorium of the Lixishe. 120 members attended. Wu Zhihui, Wang Zhengting, and others attended. Chairman Zheng Hongnian presided over the ceremony as usual.

The Chairman reported that the declaration of the Association had been drafted. He asked Hu Shuhua to read it aloud first. If there were any objections or amendments, they could be raised for discussion.

Declaration of the National Industry and Commerce Conference

408 proposals were discussed, covering a total of ten major issues.

Hoping that the central and local governments will consider the suffering of the people's livelihood,

eliminate obstacles, and promote peaceful development of people's livelihood and international equality.

The completion of the National Revolution is aimed at the realization of the Principle of People's Livelihood as the highest goal, and the economic construction during the period of political tutelage should follow Dr. Sun Yat-sen's "The International Development of China" to develop productive industries and increase the national economy as the only important plan. Now that the national unification and construction have begun, and the first National Industry and Commerce Conference is being held at this time, the members of this Association are attending the grand occasion. Since the opening on November 1st, although it has only been eight days, the total number of proposals discussed is 406, and the temporary motions are not included. Thanks to the guidance of the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, and the heads of industrial and commercial administrations, and relying on the efforts and cooperation of all members and staff of the Association, all the most important and fundamental problems currently recognized by the industrial and commercial circles, such as labor problems, scientific management problems, industrial and commercial financial problems, protection tariffs and the abolition of exorbitant taxes and levies, the promotion of national goods, basic industry problems, unemployment relief problems, assistance in the development of major industries, transportation problems, international trade problems, and industrial and commercial administration and industrial and commercial regulations problems, have been repeatedly discussed and carefully deliberated. The main points can be summarized into ten points:

(1) Regarding the Resisting Economic Aggression

Dr. Sun Yat-sen said that (the national economy and all production can be fully developed after China joins the ranks of international equality), and the abolition of unequal treaties, the abolition of consular jurisdiction, and the implementation of protective tariffs are the basic conditions for the development of our country's infant industries. This is one of the issues that this conference is most concerned about.

(2) Regarding Joint Operation

If we want to compete with foreign industries, we must have large-scale manufacturing and the latest sales methods, and concentrate capital, concentrate raw materials, concentrate machinery and manpower in order to save consumption and reduce costs is especially urgent. Recently, the match and enamel industries have implemented joint operations or joint sales in order to reduce production costs and resist the foreign merchants' hoarding plan. In the future, major industries and businesses such as silk, cotton cloth, tea, [missing character], cement, tung oil, and soybeans will also have to adopt the same strategy to cope with the environment and carefully plan for the aftermath. Now is the time for everyone to work together. This is the second issue that this conference is most concerned about.

(3) Regarding the Reorganization of the Tax System

Developing production should start with the abolition of exorbitant taxes and levies, and reforming the commercial tax system is especially fundamental. The discussion on abolishing "li" (transit taxes) has been advocated for nearly 30 years, but due to the country's multiple misfortunes and the high military expenditures, the inherent "li" tax has not been abolished, and the exorbitant taxes and levies that have been cleverly established have become even more intensified. Now,

the government has clearly ordered the abolition of "li" taxes before January 1, 1929. All industrial and commercial circles are very fortunate. There were more than 50 proposals requesting the abolition of "li" taxes and various exorbitant taxes and levies. The eagerness to abolish them can be seen from this. It is hoped that the government will implement them as scheduled to comfort the people's desire. This is the third issue that this conference is most concerned about.

Regarding the Improvement of the Monetary System

The government already has a plan for improving the monetary system. At the recent time of high gold prices and silver, special attention should be paid to the establishment of a gold standard system. However, this conference believes that this matter is of great importance and must have sufficient preparation and appropriate steps. For the present, it is better to start by reorganizing the complex and chaotic current monetary system, unifying silver dollars, abolishing the tael and establishing the yuan, and determining the paper money issuance system, and then gradually adopting the gold standard system after considering the situation and circumstances. This is the fourth issue that this conference is most concerned about.

Although the discussions about the gold standard by prominent people have gradually become consistent, I am still suspicious. Our country should have switched to the gold standard during the European War, when gold was cheap and silver was expensive, and when India had not yet used gold. The opportunity was lost long ago. Now gold is expensive and silver is cheap, and we are the only country that uses silver. If we also abolish silver, silver will become even cheaper, and the value of the people's property will undoubtedly fall by one-third or one-half. Moreover, the gold standard system requires the minting of gold coins, and the gold exchange standard system also requires depositing a large amount of gold in foreign banks. Today, with the world in dire straits, how can we obtain gold? The United Kingdom and the United States use gold because they have gold mines in their own country or their territories. Germany and Japan use gold because they have the war reparations from France. Everyone has a source, but we have none. How can we do it? So, can the silver standard be maintained temporarily? Yes, our population accounts for one-fourth or more of the world's population. If we can be peaceful every year and everyone is diligent, then the country will have circulation and the heavens and the earth will all use gold. What is wrong with us using silver alone? Moreover, monetary system theories have also been shaken, and credit standard systems, land rent standard systems, and international compound standard systems are emerging. Why not bear it for a moment to observe the changes? In short, our country has a vast territory and abundant resources, and a large population. If we can revitalize ourselves, we can stand tall and form our own style. If we cannot revitalize ourselves, we will follow the tide and rely on plants and trees, and it will not be enough for everything. All things are like this, and the monetary system is just one example.

Passing the Declaration

The Chairman said that the declaration of the Association includes all the proposals of the Association. If there are no objections, it will be considered passed.

Organization

International Trade Association

Gao Bingfang reported that the General Meeting decided to organize the International Trade Association. Members will be appointed by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and announced before the closing ceremony. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce appointed 89 people, including Zhang Gongquan (the list is detailed separately), as members of the International Trade Association in accordance with this resolution. Gao finished his report and took a five-minute break to hold the closing ceremony.

(5) Regarding Scientific Management and Industrial Rationalization

Our country's industry is backward, and it is not enough to implement scientific management and industrial rationalization to save and develop it. This conference, in view of the fact that the development of industry and commerce in the United States and Germany is due to the prevalence of scientific management and rationalization, proposes that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce invite the relevant agencies in charge of industrial and commercial administration, important domestic academic organizations, professional organizations, and labor representatives to form a National Industrial Rationalization Research Association and expand the China Industrial and Commercial Management Association to establish branches in various provinces and cities in order to reform the economic organization and increase productivity. There is no other way to change the direction of events and make a fresh start. This is the fifth issue that this conference is most concerned about.

(6) Regarding Basic Industries

Basic industries are the mother of general industrial development. Therefore, if we want to develop industry, we must first pay attention to the revitalization of basic industries. This conference unanimously resolved to request the government to implement the pre-planned basic industry projects such as acid-base, iron, coal, cotton, and wool in the shortest possible time. Other industries such as paper, sugar, and rayon should also be considered and encouraged in many ways so that they can catch up and see the results together. This is the sixth issue that this conference is most concerned about.

(7) Regarding Indigenous Industries

In recent years, our country's indigenous industries have been declining day by day, and the products made by Europeans and Americans are also called "relics." The products are of limited production and cannot be sold overseas. If we want to save them, we should use scientific methods to improve technology and increase production. This is the seventh issue that this conference is most concerned about.

(8) Regarding Labor Welfare

Dr. Sun Yat-sen said that (China's problem is poverty, so we should develop resources to enrich it). He also said that (the full development of productivity gives workers the opportunity to improve their living conditions). In impoverished China, if China's production cannot be developed, then the livelihoods of male, female, or child laborers cannot be improved. Therefore, the efforts of the Kuomintang to awaken the masses and the rise of the revolutionary masses are fundamentally aimed at developing China's industry, not destroying China's industry, and at building the order of production, not destroying the order of production. The leaders of the party have spoken deeply. Therefore, the interests of labor and capital are consistent, and the sincere cooperation and common prosperity of both parties are the first requirement for labor-capital harmony. This is the eighth issue that this conference is most concerned about.

(9) Regarding Unemployment Problems

Looking around our country's society, the number of unemployed people due to the decline in production is unknown. If we want to provide relief, there is no other way than to seek the development of production. Protecting the investment interests of Chinese and foreigners, consolidating industrial and commercial financial undertakings, encouraging emerging industries, promoting vocational education, organizing unemployment insurance, and promoting job placement are particularly urgent. This is the ninth issue that this conference is most concerned about.

(10) Regarding International Trade

In the domestic market, our country should do its best to compete with foreign goods. In the foreign market, we should strive to export in large quantities in order to further promote the movement to promote national goods. In order to achieve this goal, we must gather practical knowledge and make careful plans, expand international exchange banks, establish foreign shipping businesses, dispatch commercial commissioners, and establish international trade associations are important measures that address both the root and the symptoms. This is the tenth issue that this conference is most concerned about.

In short, the national economic organization is a large organic whole. If we want to fully develop this organic whole, we must rely on the common efforts of the entire nation. In this common effort, our industrial and commercial circles are the strong backbone, and active [missing character] must be carried out without delay. Only when the government and the people sincerely work together can we achieve complete success. It is hoped that our central and local governments will consider

Closing Ceremony

Chairman Zheng's Closing Remarks

Thanks to the members and all sectors of society.

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce should implement the resolutions.

The closing ceremony was held at 10:00 a.m. Chairman Zheng Hongnian performed the ceremony as usual and then delivered the closing remarks, saying that this was the first National Industry and Commerce Conference. Leaders and experts from all industrial and commercial circles and representatives from 28 provinces and regions attended. This was the first National Industry and Commerce Conference to implement national unification since the establishment of the conference. The more than 400 proposals were objectively and meticulously discussed by the members and can be used as the basis for the development of industry and commerce by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce in the future. The relevant agencies of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce should implement the resolutions with all their strength, and the results of the implementation should be reported to the public on this day next year. The most gratifying thing is that this resolution is based entirely on the Principle of People's Livelihood. The members came from afar, and the hospitality was inadequate. The news media worked hard at the conference and were very busy. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce expressed its apologies. All the staff and the staff of the Lixishe helped diligently. On behalf of the conference, I would like to express my sincere thanks.

Speeches by Guests

Wu Zhihui's Speech

Advocating the Significance of an Industrial and Commercial Society

The Importance of the People's Livelihood Principle

Mr. Wu said that he was an outsider to industry and commerce. Today, he offers an outsider's perspective in the hopes of eliciting a smile from everyone and celebrating the success of the conference. He has been advocating for an industrial and commercial society since his time in Lyon, believing that China cannot implement the People's Livelihood Principle without entering an industrial and commercial society. The People's Rights Principle is like building the frame of a house, while the realization of the People's Livelihood Principle is the actual construction. An industrial and commercial society is the necessary process for building that house. The "people" in People's Livelihood refers to the people of society. Humankind is born from the universe, and by nature, creation is the greatest ability of all things. People's Livelihood is based on this idea. In the fourth lecture on People's Livelihood, the Leader said that humans not only eat, but also want to eat well, comfortably, and well. Good eating depends on the social environment of the time. Human desires are endless, and industrial and commercial societies arise in response to these needs. In addition to equal land rights, the People's Livelihood Principle also aims to regulate capital. Regulation does not mean restriction, but rather to ensure proper distribution of capital to develop capital. The power of money is not the cause but the result. Humankind's needs generate value, from value comes money, from money comes power, and from power comes an industrial and commercial society. Regulating capital prevents selfishness and encourages capital development, not for the sake of capital itself or to leave it to descendants, but to develop enterprises. The development of enterprises is infinite, and this is the driving force. We hope that the development of this capital will be used to promote construction projects that benefit humankind. Curiosity is the mother of enterprise and the basis for developing capital. Maintain this spirit of curiosity and do not lose the basis of the creative spirit of creation to seek the boundless meaning of people's livelihood. This is what this outsider hopes for from everyone.

Wang Zhengting's Speech

Abolishing Consular Jurisdiction to Develop Industry and Commerce

Wang Zhengting said that now, as military affairs are being settled, gathering national industrial and commercial leaders in one place for this significant conference fills him with deep emotion. (1) In the past, the relationship between politics, economics, industry, and commerce was too shallow, as if politics was separate from politics, economics was separate from economics, and industry and commerce each pursued their own interests. The government regarded the industrial and commercial sector as a source of revenue, imposing heavy taxes and even using force to suppress it. Few paid attention to how to benefit industry and commerce and cultivate their vitality. Of the three elements of nation-building—politics, economics, and diplomacy—industry and commerce stand in the middle. Their position is like an electric current, while politics, economics, and diplomacy are like electric wires. Because of this close relationship, there must be practical connections. To ensure the safety of industry and commerce, we must first solve the people's livelihood, and pay close attention to diplomacy after opening up to trade. Domestic politics and economics are constantly in contact with foreign politics and economics. Compared with material civilization, there is no shortage of competition. To improve and develop industry and commerce, Chinese and foreign businesses must be treated equally. After tariff autonomy, it is like shooting each other with guns. The final victory depends on whether the bullets hit the target, and depends on the joint cooperation of the industrial and commercial sector and the government. (2) Some people believe that the failure to abolish consular jurisdiction in China is a political issue, not an economic one. This is a mistake. In the past, foreigners used the excuse that Chinese law had not been improved to refuse to abolish it. Now that it has been improved, they use the excuse that China is not peaceful enough to refuse to abolish it. Therefore, there are still six or seven countries with consular jurisdiction in China. In fact, no country in the world can be without disorder. Domestic unrest is naturally controlled by the country's armed forces, which has nothing to do with the issue of foreign consular jurisdiction. The reason why foreigners refuse to give up this right is to maintain their economic policies and protect their commerce in China, so that those under consular protection can pay less tax or no tax at all. Therefore, to achieve the goal of recovery, we must rely on political and diplomatic means, and the whole country must unite and support the government, vowing to fight to the death to gain strength. The greatest purpose of Commander-in-Chief Chiang's suppression of the rebellion this time is to eliminate major obstacles in the country, resist the oppression of imperialism, and realize China's true freedom and equality, and so on.

Member Speeches

Hu Shuhua's Speech

The Assembly Gives the People a Voice in Politics

The Assembly Is Not a Capitalist Conference

Hoping the Government Will Implement Resolutions

Member Hu Shuhua said that this industrial and commercial conference gives the people an opportunity to speak on political matters, which is something to be grateful for. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce is aware of the difficulties faced by industry and commerce and the hardship of people's livelihood. From now on, we should clear obstacles and renew political transformation by turning soldiers into workers. We hope that the national industrial and commercial sector will sincerely support the central government to permanently consolidate peace and unity in order to realize the People's Livelihood Principle and equality in the international arena. This is truly the glory of our entire nation, not just the welfare of the industrial and commercial sector. This conference dares to encourage itself and the people of the country.

We should also be grateful for the warm reception and the banquets given to us by various ministries and commissions in the capital. The efforts of the press to promote the conference and enhance its effectiveness should also be greatly appreciated. There are two misunderstandings about this conference from the outside world. (1) The outside world mistakenly believes that this conference is a capitalist conference without labor representatives. In fact, China today can be said to have no capitalists. Everyone is poor, except for bandits and corrupt officials. Everyone is a worker, so I can say that we are all workers and are not considering this as a capitalist conference, but aiming to realize the People's Livelihood.

(2) The outside world thinks that this conference is just a meeting, or that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce will have some more files. But all of us here are good citizens who offer our opinions, hoping that the government can earnestly implement the resolutions of this conference. When the second, third, etc. industrial and commercial conferences are held in the future, the development of industry and commerce will be unlimited. Our slogan is: Long live the industrial and commercial conference!

Zhang Zilian's Speech

Please Advocate Domestic Goods

Commercial Organizations Must Change

Labor and Capital Must Each Obtain Fairness

Actively Promote the Issue of Domestic Goods

Zhang Zilian said that he would like to take this opportunity to express his views on the issue of advocating domestic goods while representatives from various provinces are present at this grand meeting for everyone's research. (1) The first step in advocating domestic goods should be to change the commercial organization to relieve those who promote domestic goods. The defects of the commercial organization have existed for a long time. Foreign goods occupy the market, causing merchants to be anesthetized by foreign goods for a long time. Therefore, we must awaken our compatriots and no longer be anesthetized by poison. We must unite the whole country and promote domestic goods. This is the first request of this person on behalf of the domestic goods industry.

(2) Domestic goods manufacturers have never had labor-capital discord. Only capitalist factories have labor-capital disputes, or there are workers with other purposes mixed in, causing trouble, and then there are labor strikes. True Chinese workers can endure hardship, are hardworking, and love the country. If they are not seduced and instigated by the outside world, they will never strike. This person is from a metalworking background and now runs five or six factories, so he knows the reality of workers well. This time, he is attending the industrial and commercial conference as a representative of workers. Some people say that the industrial and commercial conference is a capitalist conference. This person absolutely denies this. The responsibility of the manager of a factory or store must be to ensure that both labor and capital obtain fairness in order to realize the People's Livelihood. First, we must seek happiness for the masses, then the individual's position and happiness can be maintained. For example, since the opening of the Shanghai Domestic Goods Market three months ago, despite fierce competition from foreign goods piled up on the main roads and the three major companies, it has still managed to generate more than 400,000 in business. In the future, it should continue to maintain the domestic goods market, and it is hoped that everyone will actively establish domestic goods markets in various provinces and cities, gradually shifting the inertia of the Chinese people being anesthetized by foreign goods. This is the second request to everyone from the people of domestic goods.

Furthermore, it is not worth worrying about Chinese goods being abandoned on the ground. The most worrying thing is that people are abandoned on the ground, and there are bandits everywhere, harming people endlessly. People in the industrial and commercial sector must use these abandoned people to develop abandoned goods. We must work from three aspects: you, me, and him. Therefore, the issue of advocating domestic goods is closely related to the country's economy, and we hope that it will be given great attention.

Telegram Request

Return Detained Vehicles

No More Detentions in the Future

Yesterday, the conference, based on a temporary motion (proposing that the conference quickly discuss ways to relieve the current difficulties of industry and commerce in order to provide relief), telegraphed the military and political authorities, saying: [Fragmented text, likely describing the issue of arbitrary vehicle detentions by military authorities]. Now that national unity and peace have been restored, it is hoped that the military authorities in various provinces will care for the country and be concerned about the people. It is earnestly hoped that they will strictly order their subordinates to refrain from unlawful actions that destroy or harm transportation agencies in the future, and to return the detained vehicles as soon as possible to facilitate transportation and alleviate commerce. We, the members of this conference, representing the national industrial and commercial sector, sincerely send this telegram, hoping that you will consider the difficulties of the times and work together to save the situation, leaving a lifeline for the transportation industry and cultivating a share of vitality for the national industrial and commercial sector. The national economy will be fortunate, and the future of industry and commerce will be fortunate. The National Industrial and Commercial Conference respectfully sends this request.

Ministry of Industry and Commerce Appoints

Trade Association Preparatory Committee

Review Report

Fifth Group Third Report (Continued from Yesterday)

The following five cases in this group have been separately reviewed by members. The opinions of the reviewers are now supplemented below.

Case 37: Proposing to Promote the Production of High-Quality Woolen Fabrics Nationwide to Recover Profit Rights (Huang Zengyue)

Case 43: Proposing to Establish a Large-Scale Woolen Fabric Factory (Zhejiang Provincial Government)

Case 60: Requesting the Establishment of a Specialized Woolen Factory (Cheng Zhaodong)

Case 74: Policy Proposal for Developing the Wool Industry in the Northwest (Zhou Yichun, Yin Renxian)

Case 91: Proposing to Select Sites Along the Yellow River in Gansu and Ningxia Provinces to Build a Large-Scale Woolen Fabric Factory (Shui Ziniu, Dai Kun)

It has been found that our country exports approximately 50 million catties of wool annually, with the Northwest being the most important production area. At a time when the demand for woolen products is increasing sharply and foreign goods are flooding the market, it is urgent to list woolen fabrics as a basic industry and implement it earnestly. On the one hand, we should organize and improve raw materials to make products excellent. The main points of each case are compiled as follows:

(1) Factory Location: For the convenience of transportation, factories in the Northwest should be located along the Yellow River, such as Lanzhou and Jingyuan in Gansu Province, or Zhongwei, Ningxia, Pingluo, or Baotou in Suiyuan Province. First, select a suitable location to build a factory and gradually promote it. In the Southeast, factories should first be established in Guangzhou, Shanghai, Tianjin, and Fengtian.

(2) Source of Capital: The establishment of factories in the Southeast should be encouraged by the government in accordance with the measures to encourage the establishment of basic industries for people to invest. The people in the Northwest are impoverished, so the government should specially raise capital and gradually collect commercial shares.

(3) Raw Materials: Factories in the Northwest should use all local wool. Factories in the Southeast should primarily use domestic raw materials, but when it is necessary to imitate fashionable products, they may also use foreign wool.

(4) Product Outlets: Please order the military police and students to use domestic woolen fabrics for winter clothing as much as possible, and reward and encourage senior officials of government agencies to wear them.

(5) Improving Raw Materials: Please encourage the government to establish model pastures in the Northwest and Northeast and reward people for improving sheep breeds.

(6) Organizing Raw Materials: A wool washing factory and a wool inspection bureau should be established in Shizuishan in Ningxia Province or Baotou in Suiyuan Province, which are necessary transit points or gathering places in the Northwest.

(7) Implement Protective Tariffs: Please advise the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to increase the import tax rate on woolen products.

(8) Cultivating Specialists: Please ask the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to jointly with the Ministries of Education and Agriculture and Mines to find ways to train more specialists in the wool industry.

Sixth Category (Other Cases)

(Case 72) To Revitalize Industry and Commerce, There Must Be Fundamental Measures (Resolution) Most of the six points stated in this case are essential and should be sent to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for adoption. (Case 74) Policy Proposal for Developing the Wool Industry in the Northwest (Resolution) The five items stated in this case relate to the future of the wool industry in the Northwest and should be sent to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for adoption and implementation. (Case 77) Each province should uniformly establish industrial experiment institutes to serve as leading agencies for various industries (Resolution) This case is largely the same as cases 17 and 40 and should be handled in accordance with the resolution of the above two cases. (Case 84) Proposing to Request the Construction Committee to Approve the Allocation of the Remaining Geng-Kuan Funds to Build the Wengjiang Hydropower Plant (Resolution) This case should be sent to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to be forwarded to the Construction Committee for consideration. (Case 85) The Concentration of Domestic Capital to Develop Industries Should be Implemented as Soon as Possible (Resolution) In accordance with the content of this case, it should be transferred to the first group for review and decision. (Case 88) The Jilin Binjiang Suyou Qingde Woolen Mill Requests Additional Capital to Develop Business to Strengthen Domestic Goods and Revitalize Industry (Resolution) This case should be sent to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to investigate the situation and consider it for handling. (Case 91) Proposing to Select Sites Along the Yellow River in Gansu and Ningxia Provinces to Build a Large-Scale Woolen Fabric Factory (Resolution) This case should be sent to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for adoption and implementation. (Case 92) Please Ask the Government to Allocate Funds to Develop Industry and Commerce in Xikang (Resolution) This case should be sent to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and forwarded to the relevant departments for consideration. (Case 102) Suggestions on Major Industrial and Commercial Policies That Provinces Need to Implement Urgently During the Tutelage Period (Resolution) Sent to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for reference. (Case 5) Absorbing Foreign Capital to Develop State-Owned Industries (Case 68) Utilizing Foreign Capital to Develop Enterprises: Two Cases Re-submitted for Review (Resolution) The principle of utilizing foreign capital is passed. It will be handled in accordance with the central resolution on the method of utilizing foreign capital and the method of foreign investment approved by various ministries (End).

Discuss the National Calendar

New Year Entertainment Methods

The Spring Festival Name Has Already Been Eliminated

The entertainment methods for the national calendar New Year and the thorough elimination of various decorations for the end and beginning of the lunar New Year have attracted great attention from the community. According to news from the Xinsheng News Agency, the relevant news is as follows:

The Social Bureau Reconvenes a Meeting: The City Social Bureau, in order to promote entertainment methods for the national calendar New Year, convened representatives of various institutions and organizations in the city at 2:00 PM on the 3rd of this month at the Social Bureau and decided that the representatives present would first formulate a plan and submit it to the meeting for further discussion at a later date. It is reported that the second meeting is now scheduled to continue at the Social Bureau at 2:00 PM on the 10th of this month.

There is No Discussion of Spring Festival Closure: The City Chamber of Commerce

The first article of the Central Executive Committee's regulations on promoting the national calendar stipulates that the date of the abolition of the lunar New Year holiday and various rituals, decorations, and entertainment will be moved to before and after the national calendar New Year. No holidays are allowed for the abolished lunar New Year, and no holidays are allowed under other names. An order was issued by the Executive Yuan for promulgation and compliance. The name of the Spring Festival has already been eliminated and is not included in the various commemorative holidays stipulated by the central government. Yesterday's newspaper reported that the local Chamber of Commerce and the [blank] Line Association had already agreed to comply with the National Government's implementation of the abolition of the lunar calendar and set February 17th and 18th as the two days of the Spring Festival holiday. The Chamber of Commerce stated that the Spring Festival holiday was not discussed and has not received any letters from the Bank Association to discuss it. Since Shanghai is the focus of attention for the national industrial and commercial community, the Chamber of Commerce has officially stated that there is no resolution on the Spring Festival holiday.

Chen Shaokuan Personally Inspects

Chen Shaokuan, Vice Minister of the Navy and Commander of the Second Fleet, personally led the various ships under his command to moor in the waters of Wusong Sanxia. After about three hours of exercise, they rested on the sea. Chinese Merchant Ships Begin

Striving for Navigation Rights on the Upper Yangtze

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Sichuan Navigation Association Join Forces

To Break the Foreign Merchants' Aggression

The upper reaches of the Yangtze River have long been a golden waterway in China's inland navigation routes. In recent years, British, Japanese, and American merchants have taken advantage of China's turbulent times and invested heavily in seeking a monopoly on navigation rights in the Sichuan River. Consequently, companies like Butterfield & Swire, Jardine Matheson, Nisshin Kisen Kaisha, and China Navigation Company have competed to build new ships to squeeze out Chinese vessels. In the past two years, Chinese ships on the upper Yangtze have been almost completely driven out by foreign ships, and the only remaining ships are the three vessels of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which are struggling to survive the economic aggression of foreign merchants. In order to salvage navigation rights on the upper Yangtze, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has begun to join forces with the Sichuan River shipping industry to actively fight against foreign ships, taking the lead in breaking the invasion of foreign ships in inland waterways. The following is a detailed account of what we know:

The Influence of Foreign Ships on the Upper Yangtze: The navigation routes on the upper Yangtze are traditionally divided into three lines, namely the Wuhan-Yichang-Chongqing and Xiangtan lines. According to regulations, goods from Shanghai could not be directly loaded but had to be transferred between ports. Since last year, British, Japanese, and American shipping companies in Shanghai have connected the three lines of the upper Yangtze into one, creating direct routes from Shanghai to Yichang and Shanghai to Chongqing. As a result, the number of foreign ships on the upper Yangtze has increased daily. The four companies, Butterfield & Swire, Jardine Matheson, Nisshin Kisen Kaisha, and China Navigation Company, alone have 43 ships. In the past two years, foreign merchants have almost completely controlled navigation on the upper Yangtze, leaving no room for Chinese shipping companies. Currently, there are at least five foreign ships sailing from Shanghai to Yichang every week, and at least two to Chongqing, while there is not a single Chinese ship.

Failed Attempts at Chinese Shipping Companies Joining Forces: In the summer and autumn of the year before last, Chinese shipping merchants from Yichang and Chongqing sent representatives to Shanghai to contact the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and other bureaus to organize a joint-stock company for Chinese ships on the Sichuan River. At that time, seven shipping bureaus with a total of eleven ships joined, with the aim of competing with foreign merchants. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company also sent representatives to Yichang to preside over the matter. However, as the discussions were underway, military operations broke out and the ships were requisitioned for military use, causing the joint-stock company to halt indefinitely. As a result, the occupation of the upper Yangtze transportation by foreign merchants has caused losses of millions of dollars over the past two years.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Begins Competition: Now that the war has ended and the ships have been returned, the upper Yangtze transportation has resumed. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has decided to start preparations to recover navigation rights on the upper Yangtze immediately. The branch manager in Hankou and the United Association of Chinese Shipping Industries in Yichang, Sichuan River are consulting on competing for the transportation of commercial goods on the upper reaches and expanding the plan for Chinese ships on the upper Yangtze. The bureau has specially appointed Lin Jingshi and Wang Lisong to discuss the implementation procedures with Zeng Yuming and Zhu Biqian of the Shipping Association. It has been agreed that the association will be fully responsible for the transportation of goods unloaded in Chongqing and Yichang, while the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will undertake the transportation of goods loaded in Shanghai and Hankou. First, the goods will be loaded in sections, with the Changjiang, Kuaili, Emei, Liji, Changde, and other ships operating in conjunction. Once the effectiveness is evident, dedicated ships will be dispatched directly.

Adding New Ships: The cooperation agreement between the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Sichuan Navigation Association to develop business on the upper reaches has been signed. Regarding the upper Yangtze, the agreement stipulates that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Association will each assign responsible personnel to manage it. If the Sichuan River cargo business is congested, the Jiangda, Jiangjing, and other ships with smaller drafts can be transferred to the Shanghai-Yichang route. At the same time, the four new ships ordered by the bureau will be completed ahead of schedule to be added as regular ships operating on the Yichang, Shashi, and Changsha routes. In addition, a large number of iron barges will be built to assist in the upstream and downstream transportation of goods.

Investigation of Existing Commercial Ships: Currently, there are only three Chinese ships on the upper Yangtze from the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Wuxing and Fuyang of the Sanbei Company. British Butterfield & Swire has 14 ships, Jardine Matheson has 11 ships, Nisshin Kisen Kaisha has 12 ships, and China Navigation Company has 8 ships. In addition, Asiatic Petroleum Company and Socony-Vacuum Corporation also have seven or eight ships. After all the Yangtze River ships of the Sanbei Company are returned, four more ships can be added to operate on the Sichuan River starting next month.

Java-China-Japan Lijn Apologizes to Various Groups

Regarding the Xiao Case

The Overseas Chinese Federation Asks Them to Apologize to All Chinese People

After the major case of the Java-China-Japan Lijn (JCJL) ship "Tjibaenoeran" second mate forcibly assaulting Chinese teacher Xiao Xin'an occurred, the local Overseas Chinese Federation immediately telegraphed various sectors calling for them to resist all ships of the JCJL. This call received unanimous support both at home and abroad. The Xiamen Seamen's Union was the first to implement the boycott, and Shanghai, as the center of the people's movement, provided especially enthusiastic assistance. The Shanghai manager of JCJL, Ge Liai, in order to salvage business, sent Chinese manager Qian Chongfu to visit Xu Jigong and Lin Youren of the Overseas Chinese Federation yesterday afternoon. Xu and Lin initially did not want to meet, but later decided that since negotiations required both sides to meet, it would be fine. Xu and Lin then inquired about the company's attitude towards the Xiao case. Qian replied that the company was extremely apologetic about this matter. The first mate had indeed been dismissed, and the second mate, captain, and ship doctor had all been demoted or transferred. The company hoped that the Federation would set aside political issues and seek external negotiations on the Xiao case. The company would apologize to various groups. Lin said that if the company wished to admit its mistake and apologize, it must apologize to all Chinese people, because this matter was not a private matter for Ms. Xiao Xin'an, nor was it a private matter for the various groups assisting her. It was a public matter for the entire Chinese nation and could even be called a public matter for all mankind. The entire Chinese nation did not want to hear about its female compatriots being insulted by Dutch crew members, and women around the world who boarded JCJL ships would certainly not want to risk being insulted by Dutch crew members who harbored criminals and rapists. If JCJL knew its mistake, it should expand the scope of its apology and publish it in Chinese and Western languages in all Chinese and Western newspapers throughout China and in newspapers in all major ports around the world with a Chinese presence. This would slightly reduce the public anger of Chinese people and people of other countries around the world. As for what measures various sectors would take regarding the Xiao case after JCJL published its apology, the Federation would first gather public opinion from various sectors. Because the Federation and various sectors unanimously advocated boycotting JCJL ships, this boycott would only be stopped after the Tjibaenoeran first and second mates were severely punished, the Dutch government officially apologized to the Chinese nation, all kinds of harsh and cruel laws and regulations that abused overseas Chinese in the Dutch colonies were abolished, and it was guaranteed that similar incidents would never happen again, and Ms. Xiao personally received adequate compensation. Anyone who violated this would be decided by a general assembly of various sectors, and no group could independently advocate otherwise. Xu also said to Qian that as a Chinese person, you must love China. If negotiations did not go smoothly in the future, you must stand on the side of the Chinese and fight to the end with the Dutch. Qian replied, "Of course, of course," and then left directly.

The Xiao Clan Support Association Resolved Yesterday That Each Member Must Hold a Specific Position and Carry Out Support Activities Separately. The Resolved Methods and Objectives are Listed Separately Below: Methods: (1) Request the Yixing Fellow Associations of Various Schools to Vigorously Promote the Issue to the School Authorities, and then Have the Students of Various Schools Promote It to the Various Organizations and the Public in the Localities Where the Schools are Located to Attract the Attention of Compatriots Across the Country. Dismissal is Not Enough. The Methods Discussed by Other Support Associations Should Also Be Carried Out. All of Our Clan Members Were Extremely Saddened When We Heard This, and Compatriots Across the Country Were Even More Indignant. However, This Disaster From Beyond the Sky Cannot be Predicted by Human Power. How Can the Obstacles Encountered in Life be Explained by Ordinary Theories of Fortune? Ms. Xiao Need Not be Too Sad. How Can This Strange Disaster From Beyond the Sky Harm Ms. Xiao's Chastity and Conduct? Please Strive to Achieve Your Ambitions, Seek Welfare for Children, and Seek Brilliance for the Education Sector. This is Not Only the Fortune of Tens of Thousands of School-Age Children, But Also the Sincere Hope of Our Entire Clan and Compatriots Across the Country. Our Yixing Xiao Clan Has a Good Reputation, and There Are Quite a Few Who Have Established Themselves Abroad, Especially Women. The Entire Clan Eagerly Awaits Women to Labor for Society, and No One is More Worthy Than Ms. Xiao. Please Do Not Worry About Your Future, Cherish Yourself, and You Will Surely Have Hope in the Future. The Comrades Originally Intended to Organize a Support Association Earlier to Avenge This Strange Humiliation, But They Have Been Delayed Until Now Due to Schoolwork and Professional Duties. The Organization Has Now Been Established. We Hope That You Will Not Blame Us for Being Bystanders. The Comrades Have Notified All Members of Our Clan in Yixing to Cooperate and Carry Out Promotion Separately. A Liaison Office Has Been Set Up in Shanghai at the Faculty of Law on Jiangwan Road to Contact the Support Associations in Shanghai and Announce It to the Country, Seeking Assistance. The First Declaration Has Also Been Sent Separately to Domestic and Foreign Newspapers, and There Are Also News Submissions From All. The Second Declaration is Being Drafted and Will Be Seen Soon. The Comrades are Doing Their Best to Support Ms. Xiao, Not Caring About Labor or Time.

I Deeply Hope That You Will Protect Your Health and Not Be Affected by the Autumn Chill. This is to Express Our Deepest Concern and to Ask You to Inform Us of Your Recent Situation as Soon as Possible. Respectfully Requesting Guidance, Xiao Li, Xiao Kai, Xiao Xu, Xiao Hui, Xiao Zhaokang, et al.

The All-China Seamen's and Industrial Workers' Union Received Document No. 12 From the Ministry Yesterday, Stating: "We Have Received Your Report and Found That This Ministry Previously Received a Telegram From the Consul in Makassar, Stating That Xiao Xin'an's Being Kissed Has Been Confirmed, and Java-China-Japan Lijn Has Sent a Letter of Apology.
