The Overseas Chinese Federation Warmly Assists Feng Hanyue After Being Expelled and Returning to China

Will Accompany Him to the City Party Headquarters Tomorrow to Report

After Feng Hanyue, the principal of the Zhongshan Public School in Makassar, Dutch East Indies, was unreasonably expelled and returned to China, the details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday morning, Mr. Feng brought a letter to the Overseas Chinese Federation to report everything. The acting chairman of the Federation, Xu Jigong, and standing committee member Lin Youren, received him. Xu and Lin were extremely indignant about this matter, as the Dutch had abused our overseas Chinese countless times, and the majority of our Chinese people remained silent. This time, Mr. Feng's expulsion and return to Shanghai was particularly egregious. If this was not negotiated, the Chinese in the Dutch East Indies would inevitably feel that everyone was in danger. Therefore, they decided to convene a meeting of members within a few days to discuss measures and immediately organize a diplomatic support association for the Netherlands to jointly handle Mr. Feng's expulsion and Ms. Xiao Xin'an's humiliation. They also decided to accompany Mr. Feng to the City Party Headquarters tomorrow to report everything. The document submitted by the Makassar Party Headquarters to the Central Executive Committee, the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is compiled below.

Submission to the Central Executive Committee and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee Regarding the Transfer of the Submission

It is Now Reported That Feng Hanyue, the Principal of Zhongshan Public School, Submitted a Report Stating That He Was Dedicated to the Party School and Expelled From the Country, Requesting That the Report Be Transferred to the Central Government for Review and Granted Preferential Treatment After Returning to China. Feng Hanyue Was Appointed by Ding Weifen, the Minister of Training of the Central Executive Committee, on February 4 of Last Year to Serve as the Principal of Zhongshan Public School in Makassar. After That, He Immediately Prepared to Go South to Makassar. After Arriving, All Facilities in the School Adhered to the Party's Ideals. Unexpectedly, in July of This Year, the Chief of the Local Government Police Department and the Director of the Political Department Suddenly Arrived at the School by Car to Investigate. They Inspected the Classrooms, Library, and Students' Literary Works One by One. Two Days Later, the Chief of the Police Department and the Head of the Political Department, Accompanied by a Photographer, Came to the School Again and Removed All the Portraits of Sun Yat-sen, Slogans, Sayings and Writings on the Party Posted by the Central Executive Committee, and Various Writings About the Party Hanging in the Classrooms and Corridors, a Total of More Than 20 Sheets. A Week Later, the Police Department Summoned Feng Hanyue for Questioning, Which Lasted for Ten Hours From Morning to Night. Two Days Later, He Was Summoned Again, and the Interrogation Was Repeated in Great Detail, Deeming That Feng Hanyue's Teaching of the Three Principles of the People and English in the Industrial and Commercial Night School Was Not in Accordance With Local Laws and Sentenced Him to Four Days of Detention. Although a Lawyer Was Hired to Petition the Governor to Waive the Sentence or Reduce the Fine, It Was Ineffective. After the Governor's Office Replied, Feng Hanyue Was Secretly Summoned to the Police Station and Sent to Prison in a Prisoner's Car to Serve His Sentence. The Local Government Believed That the Internal Facilities and Teaching of Zhongshan Public School Were Promoting Party Ideology and Imparting Politics, So It Took Resolute Measures to Stop Feng Hanyue's Teaching Position and Announced That He Was No Longer Allowed to Teach at Zhongshan School. Although Various Efforts Were Made, They Were Ultimately Ineffective. Afterwards, the Investigation Became More Stringent, and the Summonses Became More Frequent, and Each of the Teachers in the School Was Also Summoned for Questioning, Which Was Extremely Troublesome. Feng Hanyue Was Summoned to the Police Station for Questioning More Than 20 Times Because of This. In These Four Months, He Was First Warned, Then Suspended From Teaching, and Finally Imprisoned. Now, He Was Announced Without Reason to Be Expelled Within the Nearest Shipping Period. A Week Before the Expulsion (on the 2nd of This Month), the Local Government Summoned Him for Questioning and Did Not Announce the Reason. Feng Hanyue Was Led Into Another Room and Asked to Print Fingerprints With Both Hands, a Total of Ten Sets, Each Finger in Each Set Was Printed One by One, and His Height Was Measured. Feng Hanyue Requested to Sign Instead of Fingerprints, But the Police Department Did Not Allow It. Afterwards, He Was Photographed in the Prisoner's Room. At 8 AM on the 10th of This Month, the Local Government Came Again to Summon Him and Announced That He Must Leave the Country on the 13th, Suffering Extreme Insult. It Is Truly Difficult to Endure If We Do Not Submit a Request to the Central Government to Negotiate a Solution. The Future of Overseas Education is Truly in Danger. Overseas Comrades Work Hard for the Party and Suffer the Abuse of Foreign Governments. If We Do Not Provide Preferential Treatment, How Can We Encourage the Efforts of Those Who Come Later to Work for the Party Overseas? We Urgently Request That the Central Party Headquarters Provide Preferential Treatment in Order to Enable Feng Hanyue's True Spirit of Loving the Party and Protecting the Country to Find a Place to Entrust. It is for Public and Private Convenience. Respectfully Submitted to the Training Department of the Central Executive Committee, Standing Committee of the Executive Committee of the Makassar Branch, Guan Weixin, October 11, Year 19.

Submitted to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Requesting Strict Negotiations to Draft Measures to Present Serious Negotiations to the Governor and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in The Hague to Benefit Party Affairs and Protect Overseas Chinese Affairs. Since the Opening of Our Department, Party Members in This and Other Ports Have Reached More Than 1,600, and We Have Established a Party School, Zhongshan Public School, and Minsheng Chinese Newspaper. We Have Worked Hard to Earn the Support of Overseas Chinese and Maintain It With the Help of Comrades for Several Years. Since Feng Hanyue Was Appointed Principal of Zhongshan Public School by the Training Department of the Central Executive Committee Last Year, the School's Affairs Have Improved Daily, and the Number of Students in the School Has Increased to More Than 380. Since Minsheng Newspaper Recovered the Minsheng Printing Company This Year, We Have Added Printing Presses and Expanded the Format. Chen Guanqun, Introduced by the Propaganda Department of the Central Party Headquarters, Came to Preside Over the Editing, Which is Also in Progress. Unexpectedly, the Government in the Dutch East Indies Has Recently Increased the Pressure. In July of This Year, It Expelled Editor-in-Chief Liao Peizhi Without Announcing a Reason. Pan Fengjing, a Female Teacher at Zhongshan Public School, Was Also Sentenced to Expulsion Before She Had Been There for a Month. Feng Hanyue, Principal of Zhongshan Public School, Was Suspected of Teaching the Three Principles of the People and Having Party Ideology Facilities and Courses in the School, and Was Warned, Suspended From Teaching, Imprisoned, and Now Expelled Without Announcing a Reason. Chen Guanqun, Introduced by the Propaganda Department of the Central Party Headquarters, Was Summoned by the Police Department Just One Day After Landing and Detained Without Reason, and Is Now Limited to Leaving the Country on the Nearest Shipping Period. The Responsible Comrades of the School and Newspaper Have Been Expelled One After Another, and Our Department Has Become a Disintegrated Situation. If We Do Not Take Serious Negotiation Measures, Not Only Will There Be No Hope for the Development of Overseas Party Affairs, But Also the Cultural Undertakings of Overseas Chinese Will Be Eliminated, and the Suffering of Overseas Chinese Will Not Be Relieved. The Prospect is Unthinkable. We Hope That You Will Draft Measures to Present Serious Negotiations to the Governor and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in The Hague to Prevent This Unjustified Expulsion Order From Happening Again, Which Will Be the Fortune of Overseas Chinese and the Glory of China. In Addition to Feng Hanyue's Personal Presentation of the Oppression of Each Comrade and Submission of Opinions, We Specially Request Wang, the Minister of Foreign Affairs of the National Government.

Mr. Feng's Letter to the Overseas Chinese Federation Respectfully States: Since Feng Hanyue Was Appointed Principal of Zhongshan Public School in Makassar, Dutch East Indies, by the Training Department of the Central Party Headquarters in February of Last Year, He Has Tried His Best in Overseas Education. Because Zhongshan Public School Was Founded by the Makassar Branch of the Kuomintang, He Implemented Party-Oriented Education in the School in Accordance With the Latest Ideas on Overseas Education. Unexpectedly, in Recent Months, the Colonial Government of the Dutch Empire Has Strictly Banned the School Due to the Text Case of the Party Department's Industrial and Commercial Remedial School and the Propaganda Items Issued by the Central Party Department Posted in Zhongshan School. The Colonial Government Believed That Han Yue Was Politically Suspicious and First Suspended Him From Teaching and Prohibited Him From Teaching the Three Principles of the People and Speaking in Public Places. He Was Then Arrested and Imprisoned, and After Being Released From Prison, He Was Severely Monitored and Limited to Leaving the Country on the Nearest Shipping Period, Never to Return to the Dutch Colonies. However, the Implementation of Party Ideology in Overseas Education Did Not Violate Local Laws, and the Reason for Expulsion Was Not Announced. Such Arbitrary Detention and Expulsion Is Truly Unreasonable and Oppressive. Moreover, Those in Charge of Handling Party Affairs and Overseas Education in the Dutch East Indies Who Have Been Expelled by the Dutch Colonial Government Have Been Expelled From the Country From Time to Time. Overseas Chinese Who Have Been Oppressed and Occasionally Express Their Opinions in Chinese Newspapers Are Subject to Various Forms of Destruction and Abuse. Overseas Chinese Endure Silently, Which Is Truly Painful. Your Association Was Established to Seek the Interests of Overseas Chinese. We Hope That You Will Find Ways to Provide Relief and Propose Measures to Be Submitted to the National Government for Discussion and Delivered to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Present Serious Negotiations and Promptly Prepare to Revise the Sino-Dutch Treaty to Relieve the Plight of Overseas Chinese and Rescue Millions of Overseas Chinese in Nanyang From Their Suffering. This Would Be a Great Blessing. Respectfully Submitted to the Executive Committee of the Overseas Chinese Federation, Feng Hanyue, Principal of Zhongshan Public School in Makassar.

Our Country's Exports to the United States Are Sluggish

In September, It Was Only Worth More Than 5,260,000 US Dollars. Our Country's Exports to the United States Have Been Increasingly Sluggish Recently. According to the US Consul General's Office, the Value of Goods Shipped to the United States in September Decreased Sharply Compared to the Past, Only Worth 5,261,350 US Dollars. The Value in August Was 5,900,554 US Dollars, and the Value in July Was 8,512,373 US Dollars. The Total Value for the First Nine Months of This Year Was 86,062,246 US Dollars. Among the Exports in September, Textiles and Their Raw Materials Still Accounted for the Largest Proportion, With a Total Value of More Than 2,110,000 US Dollars. Raw Silk Alone Accounted for More Than 875,000 US Dollars, and Felt Blankets Accounted for More Than 255,000 US Dollars. Inedible Plant Products Were Second, With a Total Value of More Than 1,200,000 US Dollars. Tung Oil Alone Accounted for More Than 865,000 US Dollars, and Sesame Accounted for More Than 248,000 US Dollars. In Addition, the Value of Other Goods Was Very Small.

The Raw Silk Inspection Office of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce Received a Telegram From the Silk Association of America Yesterday, Stating That Silk Stocks in September Were 47,621 Bales, Raw Silk Imports in October Totaled 65,595 Bales, Silk Mills Sold 61,938 Bales in October, and Stocks at the End of the Month Were 51,278 Bales.

Requesting Exemption from Stamp Duty for License Receipts

The Shanghai South Office of the Municipal Tobacco and Liquor Dealers Association sent a letter to the Executive Committee yesterday, stating that they had recently received a letter from member Xiangcheng Hao of Sipailou, saying that on October 10th, they paid the winter tobacco Class C license tax of two yuan in foreign currency at the Jiangsu Second District Jin District Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Office, along with a surtax of 6.4 jiao in foreign currency for the 19th-year short-term customs treasury bonds, as per regulations. However, the office only issued temporary receipts for both the license and the treasury bonds, stating that the license would only be issued after the business tax amount was verified and that the treasury bonds could only be exchanged after the association compiled them into whole numbers. Therefore, the receipts were taken back for safekeeping. On the afternoon of the 7th of this month at around 2 PM, personnel from the Stamp Tax Bureau, accompanied by police, came to the store for inspection. The receipts were presented for inspection, but the officer detained the receipts, considering it a tax evasion. However, the stamp duty on the license itself had already been paid as required. The receipt was only a confirmation of the exchange for the license, so no stamp duty was affixed. The detention by the inspector was a misunderstanding. Therefore, they specifically requested the Executive Committee to verify the situation and request a waiver to avoid penalties, to demonstrate compassion, and to ensure the stable operation and livelihood of the business. Upon receiving the letter, the Executive Committee immediately dispatched personnel to investigate and confirmed that it was indeed a misunderstanding by the inspector. They have submitted a detailed report to the Executive Committee, hoping that the Executive Committee will review and implement it, which would be greatly appreciated.

The Bureau of Public Works Convenes Multiple Meetings to Ban Gambling

If the Closure of the Dog Racing Track is Decided

Authorization Will be Granted to the Bureau of Public Works for Execution

However, the Method Will Not Be Announced Temporarily

The Shanghai Times reported that the Police Committee of the Bureau of Public Works convened a meeting on Thursday of this week to consider the issue of banning gambling within the Settlement, with particular focus on dog racing gambling. The meeting also touched upon various forms of commercialized gambling in Shanghai and drafted several measures to be submitted to the Board of Directors of the Bureau of Public Works for review. It is reported that the Board of Directors will hold a meeting next Wednesday to discuss the matter, and a resolution is expected to be reached on that day. The Police Committee's proposals have not yet been released, but with the strong advocacy of banning gambling by Chief of Police, Mr. E.W. Everson, and the unwavering support of the British and Japanese Consuls, the Police Committee has approved the ban of all forms of gambling in the Settlement. It is said that Mr. Everson also attended Thursday's meeting, along with Mr. Fessenden, Mr. Hubbard, Mr. Fukushima, and two Chinese directors. If the Board of Directors decides to close the dog racing track at its meeting next Wednesday, there will certainly be effective measures. It is said that British officials and legal institutions in the city are planning to lend their full support. It is expected that the two Japanese directors and five Chinese directors on the Board of Directors will oppose the continued operation of the dog racing track during the voting process, while other directors may express sympathy. If the closure of the dog racing track can be decided at the next meeting, the Bureau of Public Works will be authorized to implement the ban with the necessary methods. As for the specific methods of enforcement, inquiries to officials of the Bureau of Public Works yesterday yielded no information due to a desire not to reveal the nature of the plan.

Case of Mother and Daughter Hanging Themselves

Record of Interrogation of Liu Yingzhou

Prosecutor Indicts for Abandonment

During Interrogation, Liu Still Tries to Deny Everything

Closing Arguments Concluded Yesterday; Verdict Awaited

In the case of Liu Zhou-shi, the wife of Liu Yingzhou, a native of Dongting Mountain, and their daughter, Yun'e, who hanged themselves at No. 6 Maoxing Lane, Fumin Road, Liu Yingzhou was sued by Zhou Qifeng, Zhou-shi's brother. After investigation, the prosecutor concluded the case and filed a public indictment against Liu Yingzhou for abandonment under Article 310 of the criminal law. The trial was held yesterday morning at 10 a.m. by Judge Zhao Yongzhou. Liu Yingzhou testified that he was 35 years old, a native of Dongshan, Dongting, and engaged in the silk and satin business. Liu Zhou-shi was his legal wife, 36 years old, and Liu Yun'e was his daughter, 11 years old. He had been married for 14 years and only had this daughter. He also had a concubine, Yu-shi, for 10 years, who had borne him a son who had since died. His wife usually lived in their hometown, while his concubine lived in Dadongmen. Zhou-shi came to Shanghai last March and again in May, but he sent her back to the countryside both times. In August, she came to Shanghai again, first staying at Qiaojia Bang Xundao Street. Yun'e lived with her mother, and the monthly rent was 8 yuan, 5 dou of rice, and another 15 yuan for other expenses. She liked to play mahjong and was unreasonable. She was once arrested for playing mahjong by the police of a certain district and was bailed out by him. Less than three days after he visited her, the landlord came to inform him that she had swallowed a gold ring and was sent to Qu Zhibu Hospital on August 28th (lunar calendar). Seven days later, she was discharged from the hospital. Three days later, she swallowed another gold ring and was sent to the same hospital. The doctor said it was a scare tactic and there was no sign that she had actually swallowed anything. Therefore, he asked the hospital to let the mother and daughter stay for a few more days because Yun'e had also swallowed a gold ring, and he was busy and unable to stay with them. More than ten days later, because he could not live in peace and do business, he hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit in the civil court, requesting a separation and was willing to pay alimony in court. The court hearing was scheduled for October 24th, and the summons was delivered on the 21st. She had already been discharged from the hospital because she was causing trouble in the hospital and had a nervous breakdown. However, he did not know that she had been discharged. On the 22nd, she and her daughter hanged themselves. He did not know until 9 p.m. when her brother came to find him. Zhou Qifeng testified that he was 31 years old, a native of Dongting Mountain, and worked as a partner in the Jinlun Silk Factory. Liu Zhou-shi was his elder sister, and Yun'e was his niece. The two of them hanged themselves on October 22nd, and no one informed him. Two days before her death, she went to his cousin's house and said that the weather was cold and no one was sending her clothes, so she left the hospital and said that life was bitter and she would rather go home. She said that she would be back tomorrow. He told her she should say goodbye to her mother-in-law and husband, but she said that she would be back in a week. Therefore, they sent her to her mother-in-law, but the mother-in-law refused to take her in. The next day, she brought the copy of Liu Yingzhou's lawsuit and cried. He advised her, but she said that her husband had framed her in the mahjong game and was now going to sue her. However, Liu knew that she was playing mahjong and did not dissuade her. The fine was paid by him. However, in August of last year, his sister was living on Xundao Street when she lost a front tooth. He went to negotiate, and the defendant wrote a statement promising 18 yuan a month for his sister's living expenses, but he did not fulfill this. So, this spring, she came again, first living at Hongqiao Tou, but she could not make ends meet, so she took red-headed matches in April. Now she died at No. 6 Maoxing Lane. She often lived by borrowing clothes and money. In total, she attempted suicide four times. The summons was the last straw. At this point, it was already noon, and the judge ordered a recess until 2 p.m. for the trial to continue. Witness Weng Zilin testified that he was 43 years old, a native of Dongting Mountain, and worked at He Hengchang Silk Store in Xiaodongmen. Liu Yingzhou was his cousin, and Zhou Qifeng's side was his wife's family. The fine for the deceased playing mahjong was 20 yuan. Liu Yingzhou gave him 20 yuan, and Zhou Qifeng gave him 5 yuan to pay. He did not know about the gold swallowing or hanging. Landlord Cheng Wu-xiu testified that she was 24 years old and lived at No. 6 Maoxing Lane. When Liu Zhou-shi hanged herself, she accompanied her mother to the Wing On Company. She only found out when she returned home in the evening. She did not know why she died and had never said anything to her. Neighbor Weng Yanling testified that he was 39 years old, a native of Ningbo, and lived at No. 2 Maoxing Lane. He did not know about the affairs inside No. 6. He was often away doing business. Later, because no one claimed the body, Zhang from the soy sauce shop and his wife made a public statement. However, he himself did not understand. Wang Zhige testified that he was 32 years old, a native of Nanxiang, and traded in silk and satin in Tanzi Lane. Liu Yingzhou was a friend. He had advised Liu Zhou-shi when she swallowed the gold ring. He did not know whether the couple was doing well. Of course, Liu provided the monthly living expenses. At this point, Prosecutor Wu Shixin presented his closing arguments, stating that the defendant's abandonment of his wife and daughter led to their suicide. The plaintiff's testimony was clear, and the prosecutor had also conducted a very detailed investigation. He requested that the court rule in accordance with the indictment. The defendant's defense lawyer claimed that abandonment only applies to those who are unable to support themselves. The deceased were not unable to live and their livelihood had not been cut off, so he requested that the court declare the defendant not guilty. The judge concluded the debate and scheduled the verdict for next Tuesday, and the defendant was remanded in custody.

A Woman's Cruelty

Using a Fire Tongs to Scald Her Maid

Min Mei-shi Cannot Escape the Law

Sentenced to Seven Months in Prison

Min Mei-shi, a woman from Huzhou residing at No. 1273 Xinzha Road, is 67 years old and very violent. She often abused her 14-year-old maid, Zhang Lanxiang, who is from Changzhou. At around 2 p.m. the day before yesterday, she used the pretext of an offense to severely beat Zhang, and then used fire tongs to scald her waist, causing her to cry out in pain and run away. She fled to the residence of Zhang Tang-shi, a maid at No. 35 Anle Lane, Jing'an Temple Road, and told her the story, asking for help. Zhang helped Zhang send Zhang to the Ji Liang Institute, which then transferred her to the Xinzha Police Station. After questioning her, the head of the police station learned the details and immediately ordered Bao Tan Gao Yanrong to arrest Min Mei-shi and detain her at the police station. Zhang was sent to Renji Hospital for an examination, which confirmed that she had been injured. Yesterday morning, she was sent to the Second Criminal Court of the Special District District Court. Li Zhishan, a lawyer for the police station, stated the case and said that the police station was accusing the defendant, Min Mei-shi, of committing crimes under Article 294 of the criminal law for inflicting serious injury that could cause death. However, it was now necessary to add charges under Article 313 of the criminal law for obstructing freedom and enslaving a person. Zhang Tang-shi, a witness, testified that the defendant used to live at No. 33 Anle Lane, Jing'an Temple Road, so they knew each other. Yesterday afternoon, Zhang Lanxiang suddenly came to her place, crying and saying that she had been abused and scalded by her mistress and refused to go back. She had no choice but to send her to the Ji Liang Institute. The maid, Zhang Lanxiang, testified that she had been scalded by the defendant with fire tongs. Judge Wu Tingqi examined her in court and confirmed that there were injuries on her face and waist. The defendant claimed that she had bought the girl for 100 yuan when she was 10 years old to be her adopted daughter. Yesterday, she had slightly beaten her, but she did not scald her with fire tongs. She also hired a lawyer to defend her. After reviewing the evidence, Judge Wu announced in court that the defendant, Min Mei-shi, was sentenced to seven months in prison, and Zhang Lanxiang was sent to the Ji Liang Institute for care.

Russian Women Dispute Over Fur Coat

A Fur Coat Seen in a Clothing Store

One Woman Takes Out Fur Lining as Proof

One Woman Says it is Her Wedding Dress

Each Has Witnesses; Difficult to Determine the Truth

On the night of the 31st of last month, the Kunshan Road residence of Polish woman Berta Bertaev was burglarized, with a loss of 1,274 yuan worth of property, including a fur coat worth 850 yuan. The woman subsequently reported the theft to the police station and requested an investigation, but there were no clues at first. The day before yesterday, the victim was passing by the entrance of a clothing store set up by a Russian on Zhaofeng Road No. 28 when she glimpsed a fur coat on display in the store. She went inside to examine it and recognized it as her stolen item. She then went to the Hongkou Police Station to report it. The Western detective, Mr. Smith, was dispatched to the store to investigate its origin. According to the store owner, a Russian woman, Ai Lishi Kofu, residing at No. 13 Tangshan Road, had recently hired a Russian, Sha Kaomeng, residing at No. 20 Huishan Road, to bring it to be made into a new garment. The Western detective then arrested Ai and Sha and brought them to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Special District District Court along with the stolen goods. Judge Feng Shide conducted the interrogation. Zhang Tianyin, a lawyer for the police station, stated that the two defendants were temporarily being prosecuted for receiving stolen goods, and the identity of the thief was still being investigated. He requested an extension and had the victim testify that she had purchased the fur coat years ago and had hidden it in a suitcase when it was stolen. Many other clothes were stolen at the same time, but this coat was the most valuable. Although it had been made into a garment and worn once, it was still not worn out. Questioned, the defendant Ai Lishi Kofu said that the coat was given to her by her mother when she got married in her home country a few years ago. This spring, she came to Shanghai and was wearing this coat when she arrived in Vladivostok, where she encountered rain and the coat got wet. In May, she arrived in Harbin and took the lining off the coat and abandoned it there, bringing the lining to Shanghai. As winter approached, she hired Sha to take the fur lining to the clothing store to be made into a garment. It was not stolen property. However, the victim also brought the lining of the coat to the court and compared it to the fur lining, and it was exactly the same. She also put the fur lining on her body, and it was the right length. Therefore, the victim insisted that it was her stolen item and invited a compatriot tailor, Koute, to the court to testify that the plaintiff had brought the fur lining to his shop years ago and had him make the coat. Ai also invited a witness, a Russian woman, Kao Sigaev, to the court to testify that Ai did encounter heavy rain when she passed through Vladivostok, and the fur coat she was wearing was rained on. When she arrived in Harbin, she parted ways with Ai. Judge Feng ruled that the plaintiff and defendant each held their own views and ordered the two defendants to be remanded in custody for further investigation and questioning.

A Tool for Spreading Commercial Information

Reuters Commercial Intelligence Department

Imported British "Nimble Report" Machine

More Than Twenty Households Already Using It

The Shanghai Reuters Commercial Intelligence Department specializes in transmitting market price information from overseas and local exchanges. Subscribers to its services, which include banks and commercial firms, call it "nimble" reporting. Recently, the company stated that commercial information changes rapidly and the speed of transmission is crucial. Sending information by manpower takes too much time, so they have imported a type of "Nimble Report" machine (Ticker Machine) from England. All customers who subscribe to commercial information and use this machine can connect to the company's central machine. When the company receives market price information, it is immediately transmitted from the central machine, and all other machines will automatically display the information without any errors. It is a new and nimble method for transmitting commercial market information, hence the name "Nimble Report" machine. Currently, more than twenty Chinese and foreign banks and commercial firms in Shanghai are using this machine.

Municipal Bureau of Public Works Investigates

Unauthorized Water Supply in Fa Hua Town Beyond Settlement Limits

Water Pipe Company Digs Road Without a Permit

Fined Ten Yuan According to Regulations

The Yang family at No. 241 Fa Hua Town Road in Shanghai has been using well water for drinking water. Recently, they wanted to switch to tap water and commissioned the Jin Da Water and Electrical Materials Company to install water pipes and reported it to the Shanghai Water Company to connect the water. The Shanghai Water Company then submitted a request for road digging to the Municipal Bureau of Public Works, requesting to connect to the main pipe on Columbia Road up to the corner of Yu's Villa. (According to the note, this part is entirely within the road construction area beyond the settlement limits). The

Page 16

procedure was considered in order and the application was forwarded to the Municipal Engineering Bureau for approval. However, the Ninth District Party Department issued a declaration to stop foreigners from supplying water beyond the settlement limits, and the municipal commissioner of the Fa Hua District also submitted a request to the municipal government to negotiate a stop. After receiving the order, the Bureau of Public Works dispatched personnel to investigate and learned that the Jin Da Company had privately sent workers to dig a ditch on the side of Fa Hua Town Road at 11 p.m. on October 15 to bury a one-inch diameter water pipe. The police officers and villagers of the Fa Hua Town Police Station of the Sixth District Public Security Bureau saw this and found out that they did not have a road digging permit for the city, so they stopped the work and filled the dug ditch of more than sixty feet back to its original state. It has not been started again since. The Bureau considers that this case has no relationship with the Bureau of Public Works of the Public Concession and the Shanghai Water Company. However, Jin Da Company's unauthorized digging of the road violates regulations and should be fined ten yuan according to the city's road digging rules. They have already sent a letter ordering compliance.

Husband's Whereabouts Unknown

Wife Supported by Her Parents' Family

Now Filing a Lawsuit for Divorce

Sun Honglan, a native of Ningbo, married Fan Meifeng in her hometown in 1920 through a matchmaker. At that time, Fan was only ten years old. After she entered the family, Sun, due to his family's poverty and inability to support his wife, sent Fan to her parents' family to be supported, while he left Ningbo to Shanghai to make a living. However, after arriving in Shanghai, he willingly degenerated. In January 1924, he was charged by the court for impersonating a cigarette tax bureau inspector and committing fraud, and was sentenced to one year in prison. After his release, he returned home and sold his property, and then came to Shanghai again. He was recommended to work in a cigarette factory in Pudong, but soon relapsed and stole goods from the factory and fled. Since then, his whereabouts have been unknown, and he has been living off borrowing and wandering in foreign lands. Fan's mother's family, with many mouths to feed, an elderly mother, and an aging brother, were unable to take care of her. They asked Fan to return to her husband's family to lighten their burden. Fan had no choice but to come to Shanghai to find her husband, but after three years, there was no trace of him. Fan, now in her thirties, is unwilling to wait any longer and hired lawyer Wang Liangqing to file a lawsuit for divorce in the Special District District Court. Yesterday morning, Judge Yang Yi held a hearing. The defendant, Sun Honglan, could not be served because he was said to have joined the army. Judge Yang appointed lawyer Lu Qi as the special agent for the defendant to protect his legal rights. First, Fan Meifeng stated the process that her husband had abandoned her for several years and his whereabouts were now unknown, requesting permission to divorce. Then, the lawyers of both parties debated, and finally, Prosecutor Xu came to court to argue that the reasons stated by the plaintiff for requesting a divorce were in accordance with the law and asked the judge to rule according to law. Judge Yang then announced that the case would be scheduled for sentencing at 10 a.m. on the 14th.

Flower Arrangement Society to Hold

Grand China Chrysanthemum Exhibition

Recently, chrysanthemums have been blooming and autumn flowers are competing for beauty. Elegant people and hermits have gatherings for flower viewing. The Shanghai Flower Arrangement Society's chrysanthemum exhibition is scheduled to be held at the Grand China Hotel in West Shanghai on the 12th and 13th. The society is an organization for Chinese and foreign flower lovers. It was established early on, and the first chrysanthemum exhibition was held in 1887. Since then, it has been held annually and has gained a great reputation for its many excellent varieties. Four years ago, the Japanese cross chrysanthemum was introduced, which is rare in Shanghai. This year's famous flowers are scheduled to be displayed in the grand ballroom and the Italian garden, and there will be dinners and dances to add to the fun. The exhibition will be open to the public from 4 p.m. every day, and music will be played from 8 p.m. to accompany the dance. The judging of famous flowers will begin at 11 a.m. on the 12th. In addition, there will be two competitions for dining table displays and tea table displays, so that Chinese and foreign gentlemen and ladies can present their ingenuity and compete for novelty and skill in arranging famous flowers. The audience will vote to determine the winners. All members and non-members can participate in this display. The flowers on display do not have to be grown by themselves, but they must contact Mrs. Jin at No. 70 Du Mei Road in advance.

Variety of Chrysanthemums at the Municipal Horticultural Farm Exhibition

Details of the arrangement in the Pudong Chrysanthemum Exhibition have been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. A reporter yesterday visited a certain gentleman who had a preference for Tao Yuanming and was told the classification of the chrysanthemum varieties at the exhibition, which is recorded below. The varieties on display at the exhibition include common ones such as lotus petal chrysanthemums, such as white lotus petals, red lotus petals, honey-colored lotus petals, pink-backed lotus petals, and those with osmanthus stamens in the middle, such as golden plate holding osmanthus, ice plate holding osmanthus, purple plate holding osmanthus, vermilion plate holding osmanthus, hibiscus holding osmanthus, osmanthus fragrance drifting, etc. The ribbon types include new Kirin ribbon, old Kirin ribbon, Guanyin ribbon, butterfly ribbon, white jade ribbon, peach blossom ribbon, gilded ribbon, Yuanbao ribbon. Spherical chrysanthemums include rouge ball, gilded ball, pink ball, golden dragon ball, jade dragon ball, snow lion ball. Needle-shaped chrysanthemums include red jujube needle, white pine needle, yellow pine needle, purple pine needle, silver-red pine needle, honey-colored pine needle. Among the rare varieties are the whisker-shaped flower crowns such as black mouse whisker, pink whisker, brown whisker, yellow dragon whisker, white dragon whisker. Flowers with hooked petals include agarwood hook, golden hair hook. Flowers with petals bent like rings include mud fragrance ring, white king ring, peach red set ring, golden set ring. In addition, there are various woolly chrysanthemums in red, white, green, yellow, and concubine colors. It is not only difficult to find seeds, but also the proper cultivation of the branches, stems, and leaves is sufficient to show the current chrysanthemum technology. In addition, there are pear fragrance chrysanthemum, black lotus, mandarin duck brocade, Wushan snow, green dress red gauze, red pink golden lotus, plum snow competition spring, etc. The types are not only special, but the names are also very elegant. There are too many to list them all. On the morning of this day, the weather was overcast and rainy, and there were many visitors near Pudong. The weather gradually cleared in the afternoon, and the tourists were extremely crowded. In order to give tourists the best experience, the exhibition is planned to be extended to the 12th, the birthday of the Prime Minister, so that various institutions in the city can still visit on holidays. The exhibits of all public and private gardens will be returned on the 12th unless necessary. As for today's grand event of a dinner for the municipal government officials, it has been decided to proceed as scheduled and will not be postponed. The ferry facilities in Pudong have been improved and built by the Municipal Bureau of Public Works to be convenient.

Walking at Night and Encountering Thieves Who Stripped Clothes

The Thief Had Already Put the Coat on

The Police Recovered the Stolen Goods After Chasing

Pu Zaiyuan, a 32-year-old man from Suzhou, resides at No. 7 Ziyang Lane, Glock Road, behind the cattle slaughtering company in the French Concession. At around 4 a.m. yesterday morning, Pu was returning home from outside when he was walking through an alley near Ziyang Lane. Suddenly, two robbers appeared, brandishing pistols and threatening him to keep quiet. They stripped off Pu's coat and cotton robe, and fled east along Rue Pichon. Pu then took out a police whistle and blew it wildly, chasing after them. One of the robbers fled to Xiaobeimen and sneaked into the Chinese Concession. The duty officer, Dang Chaoxuan, and neighboring officers Li Fujin and Fu Yunbo of the 15th outpost of the Xiaobeimen Sub-Bureau of the Second District Public Security Bureau, all heard the alarm and rushed to intercept the criminal. At the same time, French Police No. 482 and Vietnam Police No. 383, along with the victim, followed and caught up and brought the criminal to the Second District First Sub-Bureau. A four-inch Browning pistol with live ammunition and one bullet, a coat (already worn by the thief) and eight hundred and fifteen yuan of paper currency and four jiao in change was confiscated from the thief. Also found on the thief were two diaries, a soldier's symbol, a badge, and ten pawn tickets. After a detailed interrogation by Chief Qian, the criminal confessed that his name was Zhao Guankun, a 20-year-old man from Pudong, and admitted that he and his accomplice, Zhang Ziliang, who lived at No. 25 Zhangjia Lane, Xiaonanmen, had committed armed robbery. Chief Qian then ordered Patrol Officer Jiang Chunsong and Qiang Yude, along with Patrol Captain Wang Yufan and Wang Zhongqing, and other police officers, to rush to No. 25 Zhangjia Lane in the First District First Sub-Bureau to search. However, Zhang had already fled to escape punishment and was nowhere to be found. After interrogation, the chief of police transferred the case to the General Bureau for verification.

Thieves Captured Inside a Restaurant

One Thief in New Clothes and Shoes with Plenty of Money

On the evening of the day before yesterday (the 6th) at about 7 p.m., Chief Ma of the Second Sub-Bureau of the First District Public Security Bureau received a report from detective Li Dingyuan that Zhong Xiangsheng (nicknamed "Little Amitabha"), the ringleader of the gang who robbed Yuanhe Rice Store on Lima Road, Cuifeng Lane, within the jurisdiction of the First District General Bureau for more than 2,000 yuan on the night of the 1st of this month, had gathered with several accomplices for dinner at the Juyuan Restaurant across from the Little World and requested the dispatch of police to arrest them. Chief Ma immediately ordered Patrol Officers Tang and Wu to lead Patrol Captain Ma Jie, Li Fuyi, and police officers Shi Xunwei, Jia Tinglie, Man Zhaogan, etc. to rush to the scene secretly. The three criminals were arrested on the spot and taken to the station for interrogation. The Zhong suspect stated his name was Xiang, 24 years old, a native of Changzhou, currently residing in Wu Family Lane, Xinshanghai County, and worked as a coppersmith. He denied the nickname "Little Amitabha." The remaining suspects stammered. The other two suspects stated their names as Lu Shouting, 25 years old, a native of Ningbo, residing at No. 142 Anren Bridge and working as a牌作, and Yao Shuangxi, 25 years old, a native of Changzhou, residing upstairs at the Wang Family Stove Coppersmith and engaged in the electroplating business. All denied being accomplices. Chief Ma carefully examined Zhong and found that all his clothes, shoes, and socks were newly purchased, and 111 yuan was found in his pocket. After paying the restaurant bill, there were still 109 yuan remaining. While he was being interrogated, the First District General Bureau had heard the news and sent detectives to the station to take over the case. Under detailed interrogation, the suspect confessed that he had committed the robbery. A six-inch Browning pistol, which he claimed to have falsely borrowed from Jin Sheng of Zhabei, was hidden in the home of Wang, a monk at No. 50 Caojia Street. Detective Lu Anpu and Patrol Captain Cui of the Second Detective Team of the First District Public Security Bureau and Patrol Captain Ma Jie searched the house of Monk Wang at the specified address and found a pistol, but Wang had already fled. In addition to the First District General Bureau sending the criminals to the Judicial Section for verification, the Second Sub-Bureau of the First District had filed a separate report to the Director.

Wife of a Battalion Commander Wanders Lost

Guard Suddenly Disappears

Arriving in Shanghai, Bewildered and Helpless

Yesterday morning, around two o'clock, before dawn, a Western detective, 比萊, leading Chinese constables on patrol along Rue de Montauban in the French Concession, near the Small North Gate, noticed a middle-aged woman carrying an infant and a suitcase standing beside the road. She spoke with a Hunan accent and seemed lost and suspicious, so they approached her for questioning. Unable to understand her clearly, they took her to the police station. They opened the suitcase and found only a dozen or so items of clothing and nothing illegal. She stated that her name was Cao Zhang, 25 years old, from Changsha, Hunan. Her husband, Cao Guiheng, is currently the battalion commander of the 5th Company, 2nd Battalion, of the Hangzhou Garrison. A few days ago, her husband sent a guard, Zhang Yuqing, to Hankou to bring Mrs. Zhang to Hangzhou. She arrived in Shanghai by steamer the day before, bringing eight or nine pieces of luggage. However, when the steamer docked, the guard Zhang Yuqing suddenly disappeared. Based on her statement, the police dispatched Detective 比萊 to take Mrs. Zhang, the infant, and the suitcase to the Second District Police Headquarters. After Chief Wang questioned her again, her story remained the same. Chief Wang immediately drafted a quick letter to Hangzhou, ordering her husband to come to Shanghai to claim her. In the meantime, she was sent to the General Bureau for safekeeping, awaiting her husband's arrival.

Plea Regarding the Tragic Fire at Fuchang

Regarding the recent tragic fire at the Fuchang Military Uniform Factory on Rue de la République, in which male and female workers were burned to death, as reported in previous issues, it is now heard that the families of the victims believe that the factory should not have locked the iron gates when the fire was discovered. This prevented the workers from escaping, which is unreasonable in terms of both human sentiment and legal principles. Therefore, they have entrusted lawyer Yan Qiangkuai to petition the judicial authorities for legal relief. The full text of the complaint drafted by lawyer Yan is as follows:

To cry out about the tragic deaths and request a lawful investigation, with an order for compensation to provide relief: It is a fact that a fire broke out at the third branch of the Fuchang Military Uniform Factory at the intersection of Rue de la République and Rue Hua Kang in this city at approximately 3:00 PM on November 3rd, resulting in the death of numerous workers. The tragic details have already been examined by your office and placed on file. However, the great sorrow of all the families of the victims is of the utmost importance, and we feel compelled to cry out like Qin Ting. We hereby present the essential facts, highlight the urgency, express our full sentiments, and proclaim our grievances, running about until our voices are hoarse, vowing to obtain legal protection and humane safeguards before resting. We implore your office to show great compassion and grant our request to protect our people. Upon investigation, those who perished include men and women, old and young, fathers and sons, mothers and younger siblings, older brothers and younger sisters, husbands and wives. Generally speaking, the men are widowed, the women are wifeless, the old are childless, and the young are orphaned. If one were to gather all the families in one place and ask, the old and young, men and women, would mostly be alone, orphaned, wifeless, or widowed. It is self-evident. However, the fire, which caused this unprecedented disaster, is attributed by people to an act of God. While Heaven is heartless, the blame for failing to save lives lies with humans. Furthermore, after the fire had already started, the factory gates were firmly secured by "iron generals" (that is, the back door was locked and could not be opened, as reported in various newspapers), preventing the victims from escaping. They were helpless and forced to await their deaths. If not for the firefighters' selfless courage in opening the gates, all the workers in the factory would have perished. Therefore, the factory authorities must bear the responsibility, which is beyond doubt. Moreover, the fact that the "iron generals" secured the factory gates is verifiable, and the tragic deaths of the victims have been confirmed. Although I did not kill Bo Ren, Bo Ren died because of me. How can the factory's responsibility be evaded? The deceased used to rely on hard labor and sweat to support the old and raise the young. Now, the old and young have no one to rely on. The living used to rely on their spouses and children to provide for their old age and carry on the family line. Now, all hope is lost. The dead and the living are equally unfortunate. The dead should be properly buried, and the living must be properly cared for. It is customary to bury the dead, and it is a constant principle to care for the living. If the dead died innocently and the living have no way to sustain their lives, what remains of national law and heavenly justice? The public danger is unimaginable. The dead have vanished and become nothing, beyond remedy. The living still have a breath and refuse to remain silent. While we cannot identify the principal offender, nor flay and devour them to avenge the dead, we know that the responsibility lies with the factory authorities. The factory authorities must do well by the living and comfort the dead. The dictates of justice leave no room for excuses. How can we bear to erase the truth? Therefore, in addition to reporting to the Public Security Bureau, we must submit this plea detailing the tragic deaths to your compassionate office. With your compassionate heart and in accordance with Heaven's virtue of cherishing life, we ask you to redress the great wrong done to the dead and provide for the living. If you can bring life to the living and bless the bones of the deceased, and uphold justice to promote righteousness, not only the living will sing your praises, but the dead will also repay your kindness in the afterlife. In utmost sorrow, we express our urgent need for assistance and await your command. Respectfully submitted by: Peng Daxun, et al. Legal representative: Yan Lunkui. November 8th, 1930.

Wheeler Company

Increases Capital by 500,000 Taels

Wheeler Company, specializing in wireless radio materials, has been established for five years. Its initial capital was only 50,000 taels, which has increased annually. It is now undergoing a significant expansion. The original registered capital of 200,000 taels has been increased to 500,000 taels, divided into 50,000 shares, each valued at 50 taels. Preferred shares account for half of the total, with both common and preferred shares receiving an annual guaranteed interest of 1%. The company's general manager is Mr. De Lei, and the directors include two Chinese individuals.

Record of the Tenant Meeting at Qingyun Li

According to the Guowen News Agency, Xing Dingcheng, the manager of Qingyun Li, a property on North Sichuan Road, Chongming Road, owned by the British firm New Sassoon, forcibly evicted tenants after his rent increases failed. On the morning of September 10th, at approximately 10:00 AM, he ordered over two hundred White Russian thugs to rush into the neighborhood, forcibly demolishing houses, injuring people, and looting property. After the incident, people from all walks of life were outraged and offered assistance. The Qingyun Li Tenant Association hired lawyers Wang Zuxun and Xue Jiaqi to file a lawsuit with the Shanghai Special District Court. Unexpectedly, during the fourth hearing on the 4th of this month, Gu Wensheng, a member of the Second District Party Branch, appeared in court to testify for Xing Dingcheng. After the hearing, the tenants, feeling that Gu, as a party member, should not have flattered foreigners and testified falsely, violating party discipline and harming the people, were indignant. They urged the Qingyun Li Tenant Association to convene a general meeting to discuss countermeasures. The association subsequently convened a general meeting yesterday at 2:00 PM, with over a thousand people in attendance. Chairman Tang Huilian followed protocol and (1) reported on the proceedings of the first, second, third, and fourth court hearings. They then passed a resolution to address the illegal actions of party member Gu Wensheng and submitted a report to the various municipal organs and district party branches, requesting the Central Party Headquarters to severely punish him. The report is as follows:

To the Esteemed Authorities: On September 10th, the residents of our neighborhood were cruelly ravaged by Xing Dingcheng, the manager of the British firm New Sassoon, who personally led White Russian thugs to forcibly apply illegal pressure, causing injuries and property damage. The cause of this was Xing Dingcheng's greed for increased rents, disregarding the blood invested by his predecessors. He achieved his goals for his own selfish gain. However, over four hundred households in the neighborhood, comprising over three thousand residents, will be unable to restore their homes once evicted and will inevitably become impoverished and unemployed, violating the Premier's principle of protecting people's livelihoods. Xing Dingcheng, as a Chinese, willingly accepts the patronage of imperialists and engages in harming his compatriots, which is truly heartbreaking. Now, the injured, such as Miao Shela, have filed a lawsuit with the Special District Court, requesting that Xing Dingcheng be punished according to the law. The case has been heard four times, and witnesses, including two named Du and Yan, have testified and confirmed that Xing Dingcheng was indeed present at the scene to direct the thugs. Moreover, this matter has shocked Hongkou, and the evidence is clear. Our neighborhood is located between the northern section of Sichuan Road and Chongming Road. The White Russians demolished houses and injured people at 10:00 AM. Upon reviewing the reports of the October 23rd court hearing, Xing Dingcheng stated in his testimony that he took a car to Sichuan Road at 9:45 AM on September 10th, which is a clumsy attempt to cover up the truth. Unexpectedly, during the third court hearing on October 30th, Xing Dingcheng suddenly made up a story in an attempt to evade responsibility, claiming, "I did go to Sichuan Road at 9:00 AM on September 10th to meet my friend Gu Wensheng at Zhenqinji Real Estate Company to discuss important matters. I was not at the scene where the White Russians were demolishing houses. If the court does not believe me, Gu can testify." Judge Cheng wanted to question Gu Wensheng at the time, but Gu Wensheng was not present to testify. In principle, such an important witness should have been mentioned by Xing Dingcheng during the first two court hearings. Why did he not mention him? Now that he has been mentioned, why is Gu Wensheng not present to testify? This is logically inconsistent, indicating that Xing Dingcheng's temporary fabrication to evade blame has been exposed. Moreover, Gu Wensheng, as a party member, has violated the Premier's legacy of promoting the principle of people's livelihoods and shamelessly stepped forward on the 4th of this month to testify falsely for Xing Dingcheng, the lackey of imperialists. The details can be found in the Republic Daily of the 6th of this month. You must know that the lives and property of thousands of residents in our neighborhood are now in extreme danger, all caused by Xing Dingcheng's vicious heart. New Sassoon is a large company with a complex organization, with various departments responsible for different tasks. Xing Dingcheng is the manager responsible for the rental and management of properties. The agreement with the Da Zhonghua Company to increase rents was also managed by Xing Dingcheng. Moreover, he personally led the White Russian thugs in their violent acts. If the residents of our neighborhood did not value peace and had not endured humiliation, there would certainly have been casualties, and the May Thirtieth Tragedy would have been reenacted today. Thinking about this afterwards is chilling and terrifying. From this, we can see that Xing Dingcheng is a willing instigator, and his crimes are too numerous to count. Now that the residents of our neighborhood have suffered this injustice, we can only appeal to the law in the hope of redress. If Gu Wensheng could use his position as a party member to mediate and alleviate the suffering of the people, over three thousand residents of our neighborhood would certainly welcome and thank him profusely. How could Gu choose not to do this, but instead willingly betray his conscience, disregard party discipline, and aid Xing Dingcheng in his oppression, attempting to bury our grievances forever? We ask, what have over three thousand residents of our neighborhood done to Gu Wensheng that he must put us to death? Today, all the residents of our neighborhood are filled with inexplicable indignation because Gu Wensheng is colluding with Xing to do evil and increase the arrogance of imperialists. Therefore, we entrust our association to write to your department, requesting that you investigate and verify Gu Wensheng's false testimony and harm to the people. We implore your department to uphold justice and propose appropriate reprimands to uphold party discipline and quell public anger. We would be deeply grateful for your assistance.

National Products

Xiaofang Photographic Materials Expands Business

Since chemist Chen Xiaofang invented domestic photographic materials last year, he has established the Xiaofang Photographic Chemical Industry Factory Issuing Office in the Central Building on Sichuan Road, which has been very successful. Recently, they launched a new product, Aina (Ai) Lamp Paper, which has been adopted by major photographic studios and recognized as an exquisite product. Its many features surpass imported products. Most notably, its emulsion is smooth and clean, with rich tonal range. It is also available in four grades of hardness and softness. Additionally, its slow light sensitivity and convenient developing process, combined with its affordable price, align with the promotion of domestic products. The factory is now actively expanding its business. Starting November 1st of this year, the exclusive distributor for printing paper in the provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Anhui is Yingming Photographic Materials on Nanjing Road in Shanghai. The general manager for the three northeastern provinces (Fengtian, Heilongjiang, and Jilin) is located at the Liaoning Xiaofang Factory, and they are currently seeking suitable managers for other provinces, ports, and Southeast Asia.

Xinzha Road: At approximately 8:50 PM last night, three bandits armed with pistols entered a Beijing goods store at No. 1681 Xinzha Road and threatened the staff into silence. They stole 100 yuan in cash from the counter.

Lost Boy and Girl Awaiting Claim

The Municipal Public Security Bureau reported that the Third Precinct of the First District sent in a lost deaf-mute boy. The boy is about twelve or thirteen years old, has a monk's haircut, a long, round face with a slightly yellow complexion, and is wearing a fine-striped, bean-paste colored cotton robe with a green checkered lined pair of trousers. He is barefoot, wearing black cloth shoes, and is being cared for at the Disabled Persons' Home while a notice is posted to find his family.

The Fifth Precinct of the Fifth District also sent in a lost girl named Tai Chunnu (also known as Qian Chunnu). She claims to be seventeen years old and from Taizhou, Jiangsu. She says that her aunt and uncle told her to sell sesame candy on October 31st, but she took the wrong route and got lost. Her aunt and uncle live on a boat in Fangchai Port and sell yams. The girl has a long, pointed face, wears a large braid hanging down her back, and is dressed in blue cloth clothing. She is barefoot and carries a bamboo basket. She has been sent to the Women and Children Relief Association for care while a notice is posted to find her family.

Zhengwei Pharmacy Opens Hongkou Branch

Zhengwei Pharmacy on Nanjing Road is known for its especially low-priced medicines, and its business is thriving. Recognizing the increasing prosperity of North Sichuan Road and for the convenience of customers, the pharmacy is opening a branch at No. 259 North Sichuan Road, next to the Guangdong Merchant Restaurant. The interior is almost ready, and the opening is imminent, promising a grand event.

New Creation in the World of Dance

Mr. Kail, a renowned European dance expert and recipient of royal awards, visited China a few years ago and was amazed by the depth and sophistication of Chinese dance. He became inspired to combine European and Asian art to create a new form of dance. After a long period of research, he has made considerable progress and has begun organizing this new dance troupe with his Chinese friends. He is hiring young Chinese women to participate in training, offering free tuition as a purely voluntary teaching endeavor. Those who love art will still have the opportunity to participate after they complete their training. Interested individuals can report to Mr. Zheng at the Kail Dance School, located across from the Paris Theater on Avenue Joffre, to discuss all matters.

Great China Clock Factory Opens Today

The Great China Clock Factory, founded by Liu Daofang, Zhuo Jiliang, and others, is located on West Yokohama Road in Zhabei and specializes in manufacturing various large clocks, Western-style building clocks, electric striking clocks, gramophone repairs, school instruments, and movie projector parts. The factory will open today.

Fire Extinguisher Demonstration Today

The Jiqui brand foam fire extinguisher, newly invented by the Shanghai Zhendan Ironworks, has been successfully demonstrated in Shanghai, Haining, the capital, and other places, receiving praise from all sectors. It is reported that the Capital Construction Committee has ordered a large number for fire prevention. The factory originally planned to hold a demonstration at the West Gate Public Sports Field on the 22nd. However, due to the urgent desire of various manufacturers to observe, a demonstration has been brought forward to today (the 9th) at 3:00 PM at the air ground inside the Zhabei Charity Association under the New Zha Bridge in Zhabei, at Datong Road. Rain or shine, all are welcome to view. It is reported that a trial will still be carried out at the West Gate Public Stadium on the 22nd.

Sanyou Society Exhibits Rare Chrysanthemums

The chrysanthemum gardens of the Sanyou Industrial Society at the end of Huade Road in this city feature over 40,000 chrysanthemums, which have been publicly exhibited, attracting thousands of visitors daily, all marveling at the spectacle. After admiring the display, Mr. Yu Youren, a member of the National Government Committee, inscribed the words "Clothing the World, Fragrance Filling the World" as a gift. More than ten rare species, never before seen, are now on display. One flower has two colors, or the flower petals have multiple colors, all natural. Therefore, these flowers are exceptionally rare and precious. Starting today, they will be displayed in the large windows of the Nanjing Road retail store for three days, so that flower enthusiasts in Shanghai can feast their eyes.

Yan Zhaofeng and Zhang Zhang to Return to Xuzhou

Yan Zhaofeng, the commander of the 5th Brigade of the Xuzhou-Huaihai Assault Force, and Zhang Zhang, the deputy commander, came to Shanghai from Xuzhou to meet with Commander Yao and present a report on the suppression of bandits. After Commander Yao returned to Shanghai from Fenghua yesterday, Yan and Zhang have already met with him. They will return to their original posts in a day or two after completing their business.

Guanghua Students Organize Consumer Cooperative

Students at Guanghua University in western Shanghai have been increasingly active in organizing extracurricular research groups and practical institutions this year. Last year, students from the School of Commerce organized Guanghua Bank, which proved to be quite effective after its establishment. Recently, the faculty and students of the school have been planning to organize a consumer cooperative, with the aim of promoting convenience for all and promoting the cooperative movement. The cooperative's building has been completed, and they are actively recruiting members to join and invest. After the cooperative is established, in addition to providing students with necessities, they also plan to establish an agricultural and industrial products exhibition hall and to connect with domestic goods industries in Shanghai to promote the Buy Chinese Movement on campus.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the lower reaches of the Yangtze River would be cloudy with rain or thunderstorms due to a low-pressure system moving towards the northeast-east. There is a cyclone in this area and over the Yellow Sea, with strong northwesterly winds or gales in Shandong. South of Zhejiang, the winds are variable. Also, the temperature in this city in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was a high of 63.7 degrees and a low of 50.2 degrees. On the same day last year, the high was 68.9 degrees and the low was 48.7 degrees.

Correspondence

To the esteemed Editor: Regarding the news in your esteemed newspaper today concerning Mr. Yang Hucheng purchasing and transporting military vehicles into Shaanxi, specifically mentioning the dispatch of our army brigade commander Zhong Chuheng from Shaanxi to Shanghai to oversee the transportation, there is a slight discrepancy with the facts. Our brigade commander entrusted Li Ziguang, director of our office in Hankou, to purchase a car. The car has already been bought, and Li indeed asked Mr. Zhong to find a way to transport it to Hankou. Furthermore, Mr. Zhong is not our army brigade commander. Fearing the spread of misinformation, we are sending this letter to your esteemed newspaper for clarification and request immediate correction. Respectfully, Representative Hu Yimin of the Seventh Army, November 8th.

To the esteemed Editor: In the local news section of your newspaper on the 7th of this month, regarding the banking sector's regulations for the New Year holiday, it was mentioned that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Banking Association had already resolved to abolish the lunar calendar in accordance with the National Government's order, and designated February 17th and 18th as the Spring Festival holiday, with two days of closure. Upon investigation, our Chamber has not discussed the so-called Spring Festival holiday matter, nor has it received any letter from the Banking Association to consult on the New Year holiday. The National Government has already made regulations, so there is no need for our Chamber to discuss it separately. Please publish this letter in the "Correspondence" section of your esteemed newspaper to reflect the truth, for which we would be most grateful. To the Shenbao Newspaper Office, Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, November 8th.
